Central Political Conference 68

The 217th Meeting

The Central Political Conference held its 217th meeting this morning (26th) at 8 a.m. The attending committee members were Lin Sen, Hu Hanmin, Gu Yingfen, Ye Chucang, Wang Chongxian, Tan Yankai, Li Yuying, Zhang Renjie, He Yingqin, Sun Ke, Chen Guofu, and Shao Liz. The observers were Li Wenfan, Fang Juehui, Jiao Yitang, Enhebatou, Wang Zhengting, Liu Jiwen, Chen Lifu, Zeng Yangfu, Zhu Peide, Shao Yuanchong, Kong Xiangxi, Liu Luyin, and Liu Wendao. The chairman was Tan Yankai. The matters discussed were as follows: (1) The Economic Group reported that the request from the Executive Yuan to interpret and determine the limits of central and local authority in the third item regarding transportation was submitted for review. Land and water routes, and other transportation, that pass through more than two provinces are to be developed and operated by the central government; those that connect more than two counties are to be developed and operated by the provincial government; and those within the jurisdiction of a city or county are to be developed and operated by the city or county government. The phrase "land and water routes and other transportation" was reviewed and interpreted to mean that the land and water routes and other transportation businesses mentioned in the third item of the limits of central and local authority refer specifically to ordinary boats, vehicles, roads, canals, bridges, and other items that do not have a nationally consistent nature. However, urban telephones also fall under the scope of local transportation matters. Those that have already been handled by the Ministry of Communications should continue to be handled by the ministry. If local governments are unable to operate them but are capable of doing so, they may operate them themselves with the approval of the Ministry of Communications. If local governments are unable to operate them, they should still be operated by the Ministry of Communications. Whether this is appropriate is still subject to public decision. It was resolved to pass the interpretation proposed by the Economic Group. (2) The Legislative Yuan sent the draft of the Organization Law of the Directorate General of Budget, Accounting and Statistics for review and implementation. It was resolved to submit it to the Economic Group, Financial Group, and Political Reporting Group for review. (3) It was resolved that the Wuhan Provisional Commercial Court should be closed immediately upon the expiration of its term. All files should be transferred to the local court of that area, and the seals and instruments should be transferred to the Hubei Provincial Government. The closing expenses should be reviewed and issued by the Ministry of Finance. The question of whether the debt settlement standards applied by the court should continue to be valid was submitted to Committee Member Wang Chonghui for review. (4) It was resolved that the request from Zhu Shouguang, Political Vice Minister and Acting Minister of Political Affairs, to resign from all his concurrent positions be approved. The resignation of Zhu Shouguang from his concurrent position as Acting Minister of Military and Political Affairs was approved, and He Yingqin was specially appointed to concurrently serve as Minister of Military and Political Affairs. (5) It was resolved that the resignation of Wang Jinyu, Committee Member and Chairman of the Anhui Provincial Government, be approved, and Ma Fuxiang was appointed as Committee Member and Chairman of the Anhui Provincial Government. (6) It was resolved that Ma Fuxiang, the Mayor of Qingdao Special Municipality, should be relieved of his post because he has another appointment, and Ge Jingen was appointed as the Mayor of Qingdao Special Municipality. (7) It was resolved that Wu Jiaxiang should fill the vacancy of Wang Yugui, Committee Member and Director of the Department of Education of the Liaoning Provincial Government, due to illness. (8) The Secretariat of the National Government stated that the 60th State Council meeting resolved to appoint Deng Yanhua, Fan Qiwu, and Lin Yunhai as members of the Guangdong River Management Committee, requesting retroactive approval. It was resolved to grant retroactive approval.

Ministry of Industry and Commerce Requests Allocation of Boxer Indemnity Funds to Establish a Special Bank 69

Implementing the Gold Standard

Handling International Exchange

Since the gold-expensive-silver-cheap trend began, the National Government has instructed the Ministries of Industry and Commerce and Finance to carefully devise thorough relief measures. The Commercial Department of the Ministry of Industry and Commerce has now drafted a plan to request the allocation of Boxer Indemnity funds to establish a special bank, with the aim of implementing the gold standard and international exchange. Minister Kong has reviewed it and forwarded it to the ministry's council for review. After that, it will be submitted to the Executive Yuan for approval. The reasons and methods proposed are recorded as follows:

Reasons: (1) The silver cheap trend is sweeping the world. The use of gold coins is almost unanimously advocated by the people of our country. In January of this year, the National Government even issued a clear order to collect customs duties in gold units. Following this trend, it is undoubtedly true that our currency will advance to either a real gold standard or a virtual gold standard. However, once the standard is planned to be in gold, regardless of whether it is real or virtual, it is essential to prepare a large sum of money as the basis for reform, and it is especially necessary to have a great and stable financial institution to mediate in the middle. Japan's use of gold relied on our country's reparations; Germany's use of gold utilized French reparations. Our country certainly has no hope of benefiting from other countries' reparations, but the refund of reparations to our country should be specially utilized. According to the Boxer Indemnity, since 1930, after France designated other uses, the principal and interest of the seven countries, Russia, Britain, Japan, the United States, Italy, Belgium, and the Netherlands, still have more than 370 million silver dollars remaining. However, the remaining silver dollars must be allocated by the customs in installments each year. Now, it is planned to issue a certain number of customs gold unit bonds in proportion to this huge amount, and use the funds raised to organize a special bank, called the Gengjian Bank. From then on, when the state adopts the gold standard, all international exchange, gold storage, and gold coin minting will be handled by the bank. If there are concerns about its capabilities, consider that when Liang Qichao, the director of the Currency System Bureau, discussed reforming the currency system in 1916, there was a proposal for a loan from the United States for the currency system. If the Gengjian Bank is successfully established, then in the future, the currency system loan can be directly entrusted to the bank, which may be easier than in 1916. If this opportunity is missed, the Boxer Indemnity funds will be used up, the bank will not be able to be established, and currency reform will not easily raise huge sums of money. If the silver cheap trend continues to worsen, when will the harm to the national economy and people's livelihood stop? This is the first reason why it is necessary to allocate Boxer Indemnity funds to establish a special bank to promote the gold standard. (2) The most advantageous aspect of the sharp decline in silver prices for our country is to promote direct overseas trade. However, to promote direct overseas trade, it is necessary to establish a stable and solid international exchange institution. According to the 1928 customs report, the value of goods exported from our country was approximately 140 million yuan, of which 100 million yuan in value relied solely on bank exchange. Previously, most of the native products exported overseas were controlled by foreign merchants using the power of their own national financial institutions (such as HSBC, Credit Lyonnais, Citibank, and Yokohama Specie Bank), resulting in domestic merchants being monopolized and oppressed by them for decades. For example, silk from Jiangsu and Zhejiang, and tea from Hunan and Hubei, were all exploited by foreign merchants and could not be revitalized. The reason why they cannot be directly sold to international markets is simply because the strength of domestic financial institutions is too weak. If the Gengjian Bank is established in a timely manner and set up in major commercial ports around the world, then taking advantage of this silver cheap opportunity, all domestic goods that can be sold overseas will rely on the bank to circulate, collect as much as possible, promote sales overseas, and absorb the world's cash back into our country, even reaching the hope of offsetting exports and imports. It can also establish a solid foundation for direct overseas trade in the future. This is the second reason why it is necessary to allocate Boxer Indemnity funds to establish a special bank to promote international exchange. (3) The seven countries that refunded the Boxer Indemnity originally had specific designated uses. However, the repayment period for Russia, Belgium, and the Netherlands ends in 1940, while the period for Britain, Japan, and the United States ends in 1945. Only Italy ends in 1948. In other words, the Boxer Indemnity funds relied upon for various purposes have only eleven years remaining for Russia, Belgium, and the Netherlands from 1930, and sixteen years for Britain, Japan, and the United States. Italy only has nineteen years remaining, all of which are less than twenty years. With such a huge sum of money being sacrificed at once, there is no continuous nature in more than a decade. How about a miraculous plan to create something from nothing? Establishing a special bank, separately gathering people from various Boxer Indemnity committees, managing its affairs, and allocating the annual profits to each Boxer Indemnity committee according to the original amount of Boxer Indemnity from each country, and allowing them to spend according to the agreement. In one shift, what was previously paid with silver is now the interest generated by the silver. What was abruptly terminated in twenty years is now extended indefinitely, and the time limit is just right. This is the third reason why it is necessary to utilize the remaining huge amount in the future to establish a special bank for the Boxer Indemnity itself. (4) Premier Sun Yat-sen's railway plan once set the national goal at 100,000 li. Last year, the remaining amount of the Boxer Indemnity was originally proposed to be used as a fund, with two-thirds for road construction and one-third for river management. However, according to this method, the achievements of road construction and river management using all the remaining funds are limited. Moreover, overall planning of the country's basic industrial and commercial business is not limited to road construction and river management. If this name is used to first organize a special bank, then all previously decided road construction and river management projects, such as those that need to be advanced or raised through bond issues, can now be undertaken by the bank without any changes. When the bank undertakes such national business, such as railways, if it is asked to advance funds, there must be considerable collateral within the railway area. If it is asked to issue bonds, there must be formal bonds for the road. In addition to the interests of handling fees, the standard for issuing or not issuing bonds can be determined based on the bank's own financial activity. When finances are active, they are deposited in the warehouse and eat the interest on the debt. When finances are exhausted, they should be issued to European and American or domestic trading markets to absorb cash. In the past, when our country discussed building railways, foreign silver companies competed to handle the matter. Road A was like this, and roads B, C, and D, to the point of the late Premier Sun Yat-sen's plan for 100,000 li of railways, were all handled in this way. It's not just railways. Extending this to river management, as long as the benefits are stable, they are happy to engage in it. Therefore, with this great financial institution, in one shift, industrial and commercial industries have a revolving basis, and the national economy is also invigorated. Vagrants are eliminated, and society is stabilized. This is the fourth reason why it is necessary to allocate Boxer Indemnity funds to establish a special bank to expand road construction and river management and develop various national industries.

Methods: (1) Allocate the remaining balance of the Boxer Indemnity funds from Russia, Britain, Japan, the United States, Italy, Belgium, and the Netherlands after 1930, approximately 370 million yuan in national currency, as collateral, and issue 220 million yuan of customs gold unit bonds, named the "1930 Seven-Percent Boxer Indemnity Bonds." (2) After raising the bond funds, a certain amount will be retained to repay the originally designated uses of each related country in full for the initial years, and the remainder will be allocated to the bank's fund. (3) The purpose of the business is to handle international exchange. However, all reforms of the currency system, construction of large ports, laying of national railways, development of water conservancy and mineral resources, and various national social production projects can also be specified in special chapters and mortgaged for loans. (4) The bank, according to its special organization, shall have the right to issue gold notes. (5) The head office shall be located in the government seat or the largest and most prosperous commercial port in the country. Branches shall be established in various provinces and cities, depending on the necessity of the business, and branches may also be established in important commercial ports overseas. (6) The property rights of the bank shall be owned by all the people of China. In addition to repaying the originally designated uses of each related country in full on schedule, the remaining business profits shall be used as public reserve funds. (7) To prevent any eventuality, within the repayment period of the Boxer Indemnity, a certain amount shall be allocated and stored from the government and customs revenue, and the principal and interest shall be declared guaranteed. However, when the bank has public reserve funds, the public reserve funds shall be used to make up for any deficiencies. (8) The issuance of bonds is scheduled to be amortized over seventeen years. The principal and interest reported for each year's redemption of bonds shall be paid from the Boxer Indemnity funds due from the customs for each period. Any shortfall shall be made up from the bank's public reserve funds. (9) The bank's management shall consist of a president, vice president, directors, and supervisors. Before the Boxer Indemnity is fully repaid, they shall be appointed by the government after being jointly elected by the Boxer Indemnity committees of each related country, the founders, the Education Association, the Chamber of Commerce, and representatives of the National Banking Association. As for how the bank is organized, how the business is operated, how the bonds are issued, and how the Boxer Indemnity funds are paid, Department Member He Xikang has previously written a book entitled "Opinions on Establishing a Gengjian Construction Bank," which is attached for reference. Whether the above is appropriate, I respectfully hope for a decision. (Riri News)

New Regulations for Investigating Civil Servants for Opium Use Newly Established by the Opium Prohibition Committee 70

The Central Opium Prohibition Committee has recently formulated the "Regulations for Investigating Civil Servants", the content of which is as follows: (Article 1) These regulations are formulated in accordance with the provisions of Article 20 of the Opium Prohibition Law. (Article 2) The investigation of civil servants, except for those involving criminal matters, shall be carried out in accordance with these regulations. (Article 3) If a civil servant is suspected of smoking opium, he shall be investigated. The same shall apply to those who use substitutes such as Jindan Baidan, or inject morphine or other narcotics. (Article 4) When a civil servant is reported or accused of having the aforementioned suspicion, he shall immediately await investigation after being notified. Those who refuse to comply with the investigation shall be suspended from their duties and forcibly investigated. (Article 5) If a civil servant is found to have the suspicion mentioned in Article 3 of these regulations, the following agencies shall be responsible for reporting it: (1) The heads of each Yuan, Ministry, or Commission, or the provincial governments, special municipal governments, and military supreme commanders, or foreign envoys, shall be responsible for reporting it by the Control Yuan. (2) The heads of each Yuan, Ministry, or Commission and their affiliated agencies, as well as personnel of foreign embassies and consulates, shall be responsible for reporting it by their respective supervisors. However, for the convenience of the directly subordinate provincial customs supervisors and other agencies, they may be responsible for reporting it by the senior local government of each province. (3) Personnel of local government agencies and local self-government personnel shall be responsible for reporting it by their respective supervisors or supervisors. The term "local government" in the preceding paragraph refers to the provincial government in each province, the special municipal government in each special municipality, and the municipal and county government in each city and county. (4) Military officers of all army, navy, and air force agencies, units, and fleets shall be responsible for reporting it by their respective commanders. (Article 6) If a civil servant has smoked opium or other substitutes and voluntarily surrenders and complies with abstinence before being discovered, he shall be temporarily suspended from his duties. He may be reinstated if the examination confirms that he has abstained. (Article 7) If a civil servant is suspected of violating Article 3 of these regulations and the person responsible for reporting it knows about it but fails to report it, in addition to handling the suspect in accordance with the articles of these regulations, the person responsible for reporting it shall be handed over to the Disciplinary Committee of Officials for punishment in accordance with the law. (Article 8) If a civil servant in each agency is suspected of violating Article 3 of these regulations, and obtains a guarantee from three or more colleagues of the same level when notified of the investigation, he may be exempted from the investigation, depending on the circumstances. However, they shall not guarantee each other to avoid collusion and concealment. If the guarantee is not genuine, once discovered, in addition to handling the suspect in accordance with the articles of these regulations, the original guarantor shall be handed over to the Disciplinary Committee of Officials for punishment. (Article 9) The investigation of civil servants shall be carried out in accordance with the following methods: (1) When the heads of each Yuan, Ministry, or Commission, or the provincial governments, special municipal governments, and military supreme commanders, or foreign envoys need to be investigated, the Control Yuan shall submit a request to the National Government to send personnel or designate an agency to be responsible for carrying it out. (2) When personnel of each Yuan, Ministry, or Commission and their affiliated agencies, as well as personnel of foreign embassies and consulates, need to be investigated, the heads of each Yuan, Ministry, or Commission or the foreign envoys and consuls shall designate a place to be responsible for carrying it out. (3) When personnel of local government agencies or agencies directly under the central government in each province, as well as local self-government personnel, need to be investigated, the members of each local government and the heads of each city and county government shall designate a place to be responsible for the investigation. (4) When military officers of all army, navy, and air force agencies, units, and fleets need to be investigated, the military commanders shall designate a place to be responsible for carrying it out. (Article 10) Investigating officials shall pay attention to the following items: (1) Strictly prevent smuggling and deception. (2) Strictly prevent bribery and favoritism. (3) Strictly prevent abuse and extortion. (Article 11) If there is no conclusive evidence in the investigation of a civil servant, a certificate shall be made and sent to the government gazette for publication. If he has been suspended from his duties, he shall be reinstated immediately. If the accuser or reporter intentionally frames him, he shall be sent to the court for severe punishment in accordance with the relevant articles of the criminal law, and shall bear the cost of publishing the notice in the newspaper. (Article 12) If a civil servant is found to be addicted to opium after investigation, he shall be dismissed immediately and sent to the court for severe punishment in accordance with the law. (Article 13) If a civil servant in each agency is suspected of smoking opium or its substitutes and has been reported and investigated, the agency shall report the situation of the report and investigation to the Opium Prohibition Committee at any time for reference. (Article 14) If there are any matters not covered by these regulations, the Opium Prohibition Committee shall submit a request for amendment at any time. (Article 15) These regulations shall be implemented from the date of promulgation.

Jiangsu Province's Measures for Resettling Disaster Victims and Reclaiming Wasteland 71

The Jiangsu Provincial Government Submits a Request to the National Government for Approval

The Jiangsu Civil Affairs, Finance, and Agriculture and Mining Associations have jointly formulated a draft of the Jiangsu Province's Measures for Resettling Disaster Victims and Reclaiming Wasteland, and submitted it to the provincial government for review. After deliberation by the committee, it was submitted to the National Government for approval. The measures are recorded as follows: (1) The resettlement of disaster victims and reclamation of wasteland in Jiangsu Province shall be handled in accordance with the provisions of these measures. (2) Disaster victims' reclamation of wasteland shall first be conducted on a trial basis in two areas, Jiangnan and Jiangbei. The locations and scope are as follows: (A) 5,000 mu of official wasteland in the Danyang Lianhu Model Reclamation Area. (B) 5,000 mu of Qi Xieyuan's illegal property of the Dongtai Taiyuan Salt Reclamation Company. (3) Each reclamation area shall select benevolent and strong disaster victims from the counties in the province that have been more severely affected by the disaster and send them to reclaim the land. The selection methods shall be formulated separately. (4) A management office shall be established in each of the Jiangnan and Jiangbei areas. The regulations shall be formulated separately. (4) Disaster victims' food, housing, agricultural tools, and seeds shall be provided by the management office. (6) The expenses of the two areas shall be subsidized by the provincial government for the first year and the first half of the second year, and shall be allocated monthly. From the second half of the second year, no more subsidies will be provided. (7) From the third year, each reclamation household shall pay land prices and project costs annually from the income of the reclaimed land. After all expenses have been paid off, the land rights shall belong to the reclamation household. (8) These measures shall be jointly submitted to the provincial government by the Civil Affairs, Finance, and Agriculture and Mining Departments for approval and implementation.

Tight Security on the Southern Section of the Pinghan Railway 72

Hankou Correspondence: Since the telegraph from Yan Xishan was sent, He Chengjun, the director of the Wuhan Provisional Headquarters and the commander-in-chief of the Fifth Route Army, believing that Hubei Province is located in the center of the country and is a hub for both north and south, has paid special attention to the security of the southern section of the Pinghan Railway and northern Hubei for the sake of consolidating the overall situation. On the 23rd, he received a telegram from Commander-in-Chief Chiang, ordering that all troops of the Second Route Army in Hubei and Henan, as well as the newly formed divisions and independent brigades, and the entire Fifth Route Army under his direct command, be under the command and dispatch of the Wuhan Provisional Headquarters, and that the security of the southern section of the Pinghan Railway and northern Hubei also be the responsibility of the Provisional Headquarters. After receiving the order, He Chengjun redeployed the troops and made careful arrangements. Commander-in-Chief Chiang previously replied to Yan Xishan, saying that he had spied on Xiangwan to the south and went straight to Wuhan. There were also rumors that the remnants of Zhang Weixi's Shaanxi army were concentrating in Baihe to go out of Jingziguan again. At that time, in the midst of the changing situation, Hubei Province was not without considerable influence. Now, heavy troops have been deployed and key positions are being defended. Even if there is reaction on the side, they will not dare to try lightly. Furthermore, yesterday, Chen Guangzu, chief of staff of the Fifth Route Army Headquarters, was appointed chief of staff of the Provisional Headquarters; Zhu Chuanjing, chief of staff of the Beiping Provisional Headquarters, was appointed senior staff officer; Xu Chengxi, director of the office; Bao Zhun, secretary; and Hua Jueming, confidential secretary, to be responsible for the work. As for the Fifth Route Army Headquarters, it will not be restored for the time being, and will be reorganized when necessary. (February 24th)

Zhang Zhen's Troops Transfer to Chaozhou and Meizhou 73

Jin Handing Meets Shan En Route to Beijing

Page 10

Shantou Correspondence: Zhang Zhen's troops stationed in southern Fujian received an order from the central government on the 16th to transfer to Chaozhou and Meizhou in Guangdong to assist the local government in suppressing bandits. Wang Chengyun, the commander of the first regiment of Zhang Zhen's troops, arrived in Shantou on the 17th aboard the Fulong and Xing Lion ships. The second and third battalions immediately left for Chao'an. The regimental headquarters was located in the Huangjia Ancestral Hall in Xuecuo Lane. The troops were stationed in Nijia Ancestral Hall, Wujia Ancestral Hall, Xiguan Academy, Zhangjia Ancestral Hall, Linjia Ancestral Hall, etc. Tang Bangzhen's regiment of Liu Heding's division was originally stationed in Chao'an City. After Wang's regiment arrived, it was decided to leave Chaozhou and return to Fujian today (the 20th). The Chao'an County Party Department and people from all walks of life held a banquet at the Hutian Restaurant on the 18th to bid farewell to Tang's regiment. After Wang Cheng's regiment arrived in Shantou, it sent a battalion to Jieyang on the 18th to suppress bandits in Puning and Huilai. Recently, bandits from Haifeng and Lufeng sneaked into Huilai. On the 16th, they broke through the Donggang Township Police Guard Office. Lin Qin, chairman of the Public Security Council, and several staff members were kidnapped. The bandits have been destroying the East Road Highway cars for days. The section from Yunluo to Kuitan has stopped traffic because the passenger cars were destroyed and several passengers, including a Ding, were kidnapped. Zheng Daji, the leader of the communist bandits in Motian Stone, Puning, and others gathered hundreds of bandits on the 16th, disguised as merchants and civilians, and sneaked into the pass of Huzizhai Township in Yunluo Market. The Yunluo Guard immediately went to intercept them. After an hour of fighting, six bandits were killed on the spot and more than ten bandits were injured. Four guards were killed and seven merchants and civilians were kidnapped by the bandits. The 16th regiment stationed in Chaoyang has sent troops to suppress them.

Jin Handing, the commander-in-chief of bandit suppression in the three provinces of Fujian, Guangdong, and Jiangxi, stationed his troops in Changting last month to suppress Zhu and Mao. The Bandit Suppression Headquarters was located in Changting. On the 16th, Commander Jin received a telegram from Chairman Chiang to attend the Nanjing Division Commanders' Conference. He set off from Ting, passed through Wuping, Shanghang, and Dapu, and arrived in Chao'an on the evening of the 19th. He was accompanied only by a platoon of guards and Chief of Staff Cun Xingqi. He arrived in Shantou this morning (the 20th) and stayed at No. 7 Wolong Hotel. In the afternoon, he took the Hengsheng ship to Shanghai and then went to Beijing. (20th)

The Boundary Issue between Jinan City and County 74

Jinan Correspondence: The Jinan Municipal Government began to draw a map of the urban area, the scope of which was to completely include the area within twenty li of Jinan City into the urban area. The representatives of the various circles of Licheng County held a meeting and decided to oppose it. As a result, there was the issue of the boundary between the city and the county. Representatives of the county government and the county party department initially met with Zhao Jingshi, the mayor of Jinan, to exchange opinions. The city side argued that the urban area was set within twenty li around, based on the Jinan garrison area in the past, which is now the scope of the Public Security District, and not to seek expansion outside the scope. The county side reasoned that if it is set within twenty li, it must be east to Lengshui Ditch, west to Yinma Village, south to the Watershed Ridge, and north across the Yellow River to Balidian. There would be little remaining in Licheng County. Moreover, the western boundary to Yinma Village will even be within the territory of Changqing County. Although the Jinan garrison area was within twenty li in the past, it did not conflict with the administration of the county. If the urban area is now within twenty li and the county area is outside twenty li, there are many villages within twenty li that are included in the urban area, which has made the county administration and party affairs inconsistent. The tax revenue will be greatly affected. Therefore, it is requested that the urban area should still be within the scope of the city gate and commercial port. The talks did not resolve the issue at that time. It was only agreed that the city and county sides each appoint four representatives to hold another meeting. On Saturday and Sunday, the county representatives Wu Zizhen, Zhao Tongyuan, Li Rongfu, and Shen Kunfei went to the municipal government and met with the city representatives Cheng Qibao and Zhang Hongjian. After some discussion, although there was a close hope, there was still no concrete solution. It is said that the city representatives advocated submitting a request to the provincial government for a decision. (21st)

Naval Inspection Group Leaves the United States for England 75

After leaving Washington on January 23, the Du Xigui Naval Inspection Group arrived in Philadelphia that evening. The next day, they visited the naval dockyard and factory there. In the afternoon, they took a plane provided by the navy to Lakhurst to visit the new-style airship. They returned by the same plane and went to Portsmouth in the evening. They visited the submarine manufacturing plant there, and then took a car to Boston. The mayor of the city sent someone to entertain them warmly and guided them to see the whole city. In the evening, they went to Newport, where there is a naval academy. After the visit, they arrived in New London on the night of the 26th. The next day, they visited the naval shipyard and the latest type of cruiser. On the night of the 28th, they arrived in New York, where the overseas Chinese and naval and army circles welcomed them warmly. On the 29th, they visited the Brooklyn dockyard and factory. In the evening, the Sino-American Association held a tea party. In the evening, they went to the invitation of the New York branch of the Kuomintang. On the 30th, they went to Hancodk to visit the army artillery battery. At four o'clock, all overseas Chinese in New York held a welcome meeting. At five o'clock, they went to a public banquet of all overseas Chinese. On the 31st, they packed their luggage and boarded the Bromen ship in the evening to go to England. It is said that the ship will be expanded on February 1st and will arrive in London on the 5th. The United Press reported from Tokyo on the 26th that Du Xigui, who was inspecting the navies of Europe and the United States, met the British Emperor in London.

Local Communications

Jiading 76

Anting Township Purchases Rice for Price Stabilization: Since the new grains entered the market in Anting Township last year, the price of rice has been increasing day by day, recently rising to about sixteen yuan per stone. Hoarders still want to hoard. The gentry of the township yesterday (25th) gathered all the rice industry and wealthy residents in Tongrentang to discuss ways to relieve the rice shortage. It was decided to raise huge sums of money according to the regulations of 1926 and 1927, purchase and transport Xian rice, and sell it at a fair price, which will be implemented on May 1st. A Fleeing Woman is Shackled: Qu, the wife of Ni Axiao, a farmer in Niwan, Anting Township, was lured away by Wei Sifu, a villager, in September of the year before last. Axiao eventually found her and sued Wei Sifu to the county government, who was sentenced to imprisonment. Not long after Qu returned home, she left on the pretext of visiting her parents. Until the 20th of this month, Ni's relatives bought groceries in the French Concession of Shanghai and saw Qu walking on the road. They ordered her to return with them and sent her to the Ni family. Ni's mother gave her a reprimand and temporarily confined her in the room. Unexpectedly, she was untamed and tried to escape through the window while her mother-in-law was asleep. She was caught. Axiao, believing that his wife had not repented at all and had not given up the idea of escaping, consulted with his mother's family and shackled her to prevent her from being free.

Kunshan 77

The Detained Firefighters Released: The county public security bureau secretly investigated a conflict with the firefighters during the fire. The county magistrate Wu ordered the public security bureau to detain eight firefighters including Gu Sanyuan. It has been two weeks. Now, they have been ordered to be released by the Department of Civil Affairs. Yesterday, the county government released Gu Sanyuan and other eight people by Yuzheng Trial Member. It is said that the Firefighters' Federation believes that Gu and other eight people were unjustly detained for public affairs, and scheduled a meeting to welcome them.

Commissioner of Civil Affairs Visits Kunshan: Wu Shoupeng, Section Chief of the Second Section of the Department of Civil Affairs, arrived in Kunshan from Shanghai on the 25th. He went to the First District Office to meet with District Chief Yan Huating and accompanied him on an inspection. In the afternoon, he learned that Commissioner Miao would come to Kunshan to inspect district affairs. Therefore, all agencies sent people to the station to welcome him. At two o'clock, he learned that Commissioner Miao had gone to Danyang. After Wu Section Chief telegraphed to Danyang to inquire, he received a reply that the Commissioner was scheduled to come to Kunshan from Wuxi at eight o'clock this morning (26th) and give a public lecture in the county government's auditorium.

Suzhou 78

The Water Police Team Will Launch a Large-Scale Suppression of Bandits: Gong, the District Chief of the Third District of the Water Public Security Bureau, yesterday ordered the two warship captains, Pei Rong and Zhen Wei, the guerrilla captain, and the captains of their respective teams to depart immediately and patrol Pingwang, Lili, Luhu, Zhouzhuang, Dianshan Lake, Chenmu, and other places. They also agreed to gather in Pingwang on a certain day to conduct a joint patrol and suppression of lake bandits.

The list of officially selected candidates is as follows: Zhao Yanfang, Li Changzhen, Shou Shaochang, Wang Shufu, Gu Jizong, Zhi Dinglu, Li Yaolu, Li Bangwan, Chen Xingying, Zhang Chengchang, Qian Pengnian, Li Kegao, Zhang Haifeng, Wang Yisun, Yang Hailin, Zhu Weiquan, Yao Zhuguang, Liu Baichuan, Wang Weixin, Chen Yi, Zhang Zongren, Zhao Wenbin, He Xiongjie, Ma Yangzhi, Chen Dengyun, Liu Jinkui, Li Chunming, Zhang Wenshun, Chen Zhenhua, Hao Sheng.

Bandit Traces Discovered at the Three Taishi Temple: The County Government yesterday (the 26th) received a report from the Tian Shen District Chief stating that bandit traces were discovered at the Three Taishi Temple in Weiting District, on the opposite bank of the Yangcheng Lake area. The bandits even dressed the clay statues in the temple with the military caps and uniforms of the security guards, making it appear as if there were gatekeepers from a distance. Also, the Third District of the Water Public Security Bureau sent a letter to the County Government yesterday, stating that the 11th and 12th teams had been dispatched to pursue and suppress the bandits. At the same time, the 14th and 15th teams were dispatched to intercept them. It was also reported that the bandits were still in the Xiaojing area, more than ten miles away from Xiangcheng. The police warships Pei Rong and Zhen Cheng, due to the shallow water in Yangcheng Lake, were unable to exit and had to go around from Pingwang to encircle them.

Qingpu 79

County Government Prepares for Afforestation Campaign: The County Government of this county previously received an order from the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Agriculture and Mining, stating that the afforestation campaign is one of the seven-day campaigns stipulated by the National Government. Now that the spring tree planting season is approaching, the County Government was instructed to handle it. After receiving the order, the County Government immediately instructed the Construction and Education Bureau and the County Agricultural Farm to jointly draft a plan and submit it to the county administrative meeting for revision and approval. The County Government then submitted it to the Department of Agriculture and Mining for approval.

Young Monk Loses Both Wife and Money: Zhao Xiaoheshang, a farmer from Lingjia Village in Qingpu, works as a carpenter. His mother, seeing that her son had come of age, asked someone to act as an intermediary. This matter was learned by Dai, a Jiading native who was accustomed to acting as an "ant matchmaker" (engaging in illicit matchmaking).

Dai colluded with an accomplice named Gu and went to Zhao Xiaoheshang's house, pretending to go to a lottery gathering together and visit along the way. Afterward, they often visited Zhao's house to chat, pretending to ask where his sister-in-law was. The mother replied that she was currently asking someone to act as a matchmaker, hoping they would pay attention to any suitable families. Dai readily agreed and left. Several days later, Dai came and told Zhao Xiaoheshang's mother that there was a Zhang woman, a native of Huzhou, whose parents had both died and who lived with her brother in a neighboring village. She needed a betrothal gift of 150 gold yuan, as well as gold jewelry and clothing worth about 200 yuan. The mother replied that she did not have such financial resources. Finally, they agreed on a bride price of 100 yuan and a matchmaking fee of 20 yuan to marry the woman. After she entered the house, the couple was still harmonious, but she was lazy and unwilling to work. Her son still went out to work, leaving in the morning and returning in the evening, as was his custom. Unexpectedly, the Zhang woman took advantage of her husband's absence the other day and ran away with her clothes and jewelry. When Xiaoheshang returned home, he did not see his wife. He opened the box and found that all the valuable clothes and items had been taken away, worth about 100 yuan. He immediately rushed to Dai's place to inquire, but Dai was also gone. Zhao Xiaoheshang realized that he had been the victim of an "ant matchmaker" and went to confront Gu, the accomplice. It is unknown what the outcome was.

Husband Tries to Catch Wife in Adultery, But Fails: In a certain town in Qingpu, there is a carpenter named Gu from Songjiang, who is currently in his thirties. His wife, Yang, is somewhat attractive. A fellow tradesman named Zhou often visited Gu's place. Later, with the help of Xue Zhu, a woman living with Zhou, Zhou and Yang committed adultery. This had happened more than once. The other night, Gu was drinking tea in a teahouse. When he returned home at about 9:00 p.m., the front door was already closed. He went to the back door. Xue Zhu heard Gu return and panicked. She shouted, "You're back!" to signal Zhou to escape quickly. Gu, seeing this, became suspicious and rushed upstairs to his own room, but did not see his wife. He immediately turned around and went downstairs to search Xue Zhu's room. Sure enough, he saw his wife, Yang, and Zhou lying on Xue Zhu's bed. The two were putting on their clothes. Gu was enraged and tried to catch them in adultery, but was instead pushed to the ground. Zhou and Yang took the opportunity to escape. Gu chased after them, but could not find them. He later negotiated with Xue Zhu to demand the return of his wife, but it is said that Yang has not yet returned home.

Fengxian 80

Village Girl Commits Suicide Over Double Love Affair: Wang Amei, a salt worker from Huangjia Village in the eastern countryside, is of marriageable age. Since childhood, she and her neighbor Zhang Bangdi had been close friends and secretly made a marriage agreement. However, Zhang went to Shanghai last year to work. A man named He Xiaoguan, who lived about a mile away and was a distant relative of the girl, coveted her beauty and tried to seduce her in every way. He also succeeded in his pursuit. Recently, they even reached the point of betrothal. At that time, Zhang had an agreement with the woman, so his mother went to discuss the marriage, but was rejected. One day Zhang suddenly returned home and learned of the situation. He immediately went to question her. The girl regretted her recklessness and remained silent. She then committed suicide in her room late at night. Before her death, she buried all the objects given to her by the two lovers in the backyard, presumably to express her repentance.

River Works Implemented by Cutting Through Banks: The sections of the Nanqiao Tang River project do not involve demolishing Zhang Tan, but only dredging the river. However, the three contract workers from other provinces are only focused on the beach, namely, spreading the mud raised from the riverbed flat on the beach, in order to fulfill their responsibilities. Now the East and West River Bureaus have found out the truth and specially used coal tar bags to mark the slope of the beach bank yesterday, ordering the foremen to remove it all and sending personnel to monitor it, in order to complete the project.

Levying Sutra Repentance Donation to Be Launched Soon: The Sutra Repentance Donation, which was decided to be levied by the county administrative meeting to fund the compilation of local chronicles and education, has been approved by the Finance Department. The Finance Bureau has been instructed to formulate collection methods and invite merchants to contract for it. It is said that it will be officially launched as soon as the investigation is completed.

Wuxi 81

Minutes of the Meeting of the Silk Factory Association: The Silk Factory Association of this county reorganized the other day and re-elected Qian Fenghao and ten others as executive committee members. Yesterday, the association held its first joint meeting of the first executive committee. Important cases were discussed and resolved: (1) The association will immediately send a telegram to the Ministry of Industry and Commerce, stating that the implementation of public weighing is extremely harmful to the silk industry in China and requesting that the hardships of Chinese merchants be considered and that it not be implemented. A letter will also be sent to the Shanghai silk industry, stating the reasons for opposition. (2) A letter from the county government stated that Zhu Danian and others sued Yang Zhongtian for selling inferior Japanese autumn seeds and falsely claiming that they were products of the West Lake Seed Breeding Farm. A request was made for an investigation and reply. It was decided to invite both parties to the meeting for mediation. If a resolution could not be reached, the county government would be asked to handle it. Subsequently, Qian Fenghao, Yang Yuchu, and Xie You'an were mutually elected as standing committee members, and Qian Fenghao was mutually elected as chairman.

Director Miao Visits Wuxi to Inspect Autonomy: Miao, the Director of the Civil Affairs Department of the Jiangsu Provincial Government, believes that it is necessary to check the progress and quality of the organization of districts, townships, villages, and neighborhoods in each county at any time in order to supervise and urge them. Therefore, he departed from Zhenjiang and first went to Wujin to inspect. He then arrived in Wuxi by car from Changzhou at about 10:00 p.m. the night before. After Director Miao got off the car, he took a car back to the public hall of Bianmin Bridge to rest. Yesterday (the 26th), Miao went to the first and second districts to inspect the current state of autonomy and then went to Kunshan for inspection.

Murderer Writes Poetry in Prison: Xue Shihao, from Tangtou Bridge in the area where Cheng and Xi intersect, shot and killed Xue Picheng, Huang Wangchun, Liu Deming, Chen Ruilin, and other four people due to a feud. Huang and Chen had already died, while Xue Picheng and Liu Deming were still in the Puren Hospital in Wuxi and were not in danger of dying. The murderer Xue Shihao was also arrested and imprisoned by the Jiangyin County Government. He had repeatedly requested an early sentence so that he could die quickly. However, the county government had to obtain an accurate diagnosis from the hospital before making a final decision and had sent Wu Bowen, the political and police chief, to Wuxi to investigate. After his arrest, the murderer Xue Shihao once tried to commit suicide by hitting his head against a glass window. Recently, his attitude has been calm, and he has written two quatrains, which are recorded to show a glimpse of the circumstances of his crime. The poems read: "Layers of oppression are truly lamentable, one blow was ineffective and misdirected the car. Weak commoners are all in hell, I live in prison as a pioneer." "My family is ruined and I am dead, my grievances have not been voiced, I cover myself with a blanket and toss and turn at night. Who has ever lived without dying since ancient times? I want to knock on the darkness and complain of injustice."

Rice Boat Collides with Motorboat, Nearly Causing Fatal Accident: Yesterday, a motorboat carrying eight passengers, men and women, sailed from Yuqi Town to the city. At about 7:00 p.m., when it reached the Ni Xiangzhuang area, a rice boat suddenly came head-on. Due to the darkness of the night, it was too late to avoid it, causing the two boats to collide. The motorboat immediately capsized, and the eight passengers also fell into the river at the same time, shouting for help. They were rescued one by one by the fishing boats there, and fortunately, no one drowned. The rice boat that caused the accident has escaped.

Recovering Reclamation Prices from Huai Various Fields: The Huainan Various Fields have been abandoned for more than ten years, but the reclamation prices have not been paid in full. Fierce Battle Between Police and Bandits at Da'an Port: Five bandit boats were discovered outside Da'an Port on the morning of the 25th, carrying more than two hundred bandits. The second squad of the 18th Water Police Team stationed at the port intercepted them, and a fierce battle lasted for five hours. The bandit side suffered many casualties and three bandits were captured. One hostage was rescued. The bandit boats have not yet retreated. The team headquarters specially sent 5,000 rounds of ammunition to the port for use.

County Government Concluding Judicial Matters: The Nantong County Court is scheduled to be established on March 5. The County Government is now concluding the judicial matters that it is handling concurrently. Director Dong Banggan is scheduled to receive the case files on the 4th. Robbery and Injury at Da Wu Lane: The home of Wu Xingbang in Da Wu Lane outside of Ma Lane Gate was suddenly attacked by more than ten bandits last night, each carrying box cannons, rushing into the house, forbidding any noise, and wantonly looting. Zhenjiang 84

Jiangsu Civil Affairs Department Discusses Important Policies: The Jiangsu Civil Affairs Department held a departmental meeting yesterday and resolved the following important matters: (1) Issue a circular to all counties to strictly declare the meaning of confidential orders. (2) All townships and towns in the province will hold a regular anti-smoking campaign, to be drafted and handled by the Fifth Section. (3) This province should actively promote proper entertainment for the people, and the Fifth Section will draft measures for further discussion. (4) Those counties whose public security expenses have not yet been determined should follow the resolutions of the previous general administrative meeting and find a solution within one week. (5) This Department should delineate police districts for inspection, to be handled by the Third Section immediately. (6) Compile and print the "Must-Know for County Magistrates of Jiangsu Province" and "Must-Know for Police," to be handled by the First and Third Sections. (7) Hu Shusheng proposed the formulation of temporary measures for weddings, funerals, celebrations, sacrifices, banquets, etc., and ordered all personnel of this Department and directly subordinate agencies to comply with them in order to awaken social morals (resolved) Hu Jun will draft specific opinions for further discussion. Prison Officer Jiang Wenbao Dismissed: The Jiangsu Higher Court, believing that Jiang Wenbao, a prison officer in Zhenjiang, was derelict in his duty, resulting in a prison break, specially ordered his dismissal yesterday and appointed Xia Dingen as his replacement.

The Truth About the Murder of the Quartermaster of the Military Police Regiment: Liang Changhua, the quartermaster director of the First Regiment of Military Police stationed in Zhenjiang, was ordered to go to Beijing to receive funds for the January military pay. When he was about to leave, Wen Xiaoxiong suddenly came and went with him. Liang did not suspect him because Wen was a classmate from the fourth term of Huangpu. Therefore, they went to Beijing by the same car. After arriving in Beijing, Wen invited Liang to stay at the Asia Hotel, saying that he had already booked a room. Two days later, Liang received 4,000 yuan in military pay from the Weiwu Command. The next morning, Quartermaster Liang was found brutally murdered with his head broken and bleeding, and the military pay he had received and Wen were both missing. The First Police Bureau, together with the local court, conducted an inspection. After the news spread, it was reported to Wei Yingshan, the director of the Beijing garrison office, by the First Regiment of Military Police. Chen Xiufeng, the regimental commander in Zhenjiang, received the news via long-distance telephone and took soldiers to Beijing. He immediately ordered Chen Xiwu, the captain of the intelligence team, to request the First Police Bureau and the local court to open the coffin for a second examination. The regimental commander and his followers confirmed that the deceased was Quartermaster Liang Changhua. The murderer is now being strictly pursued and brought to justice.

Provincial Government Replies on the Takeover of Concession Public Property: The Provincial Government previously approved a document from the Ministry of Foreign Affairs stating that the public property of the Zhenjiang Concession should be received and kept by the Zhenjiang County Government. It was immediately instructed to comply with the document. According to a report from Zhang, the county magistrate of Zhenjiang County, the transferred items have been inventoried and kept by the county, and a receipt has been sent to Commissioner Dai. Therefore, a list of the received items has been copied and sent to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs for reference.

Execution of Robbers and Murderers by Firing Squad: At 2:00 p.m. on the 25th, the County Government, following a telegram from the Provincial Government, executed Wang Mingxiang, a robber who killed a monk named Yuanxue from the Jiuhua Nunnery in Zhenwu Temple Town and murdered a single Zhang woman, by firing squad behind the vagrant reformatory. In addition to submitting a report on the execution date, the crimes were also announced.

Department Order to Levy Agricultural Improvement Donations: The County Government received an order from the Provincial Government, instructing that, as proposed by Commissioner He Yushu, starting in the busy season of the 19th year, each county should levy an agricultural improvement donation of two cents per mu under the busy season silver item, but it must not conflict with the percentage method (those whose original levy has not exceeded should be levied according to the levy, if the levy of two cents exceeds, a reduction is allowed). Yesterday (the 24th), it specially ordered the Finance Bureau to list the original number of principal and supplementary taxes and submit them to the county for transfer to the department for verification.

Alkali Salt Shortage Replaced by Relief Sales: Zhang Jiarui, the Huaihe Transport Commissioner, stated that the alkali salt in the storage trenches was constantly short and difficult to transport. Recently, merchants from Pingjiang and other ports have submitted reports to the department, requesting that the salt in the storage trenches be replaced by relief sales to avoid the people eating bland food. Yesterday (the 24th), in addition to ordering the trench chiefs to reply, he specially ordered the merchants to wait for consideration of the situation before handling it.

Bandits Rob Five Families: More than ten bandits suddenly came to Zuo Jia Zhuang in the county at dusk the day before yesterday, each holding guns and weapons, and robbed five families in a row, shot and injured one person, and robbed two rifles, with losses of about seven or eight hundred yuan.

Further News on the Destruction of the Public Case by Rioters: It has been heard that in Beisha Town in this county, several hundred ignorant people held a Dragon King Assembly yesterday, which led to the destruction of the town office and the belongings of the deputy town chief Meng Lizhai. The county government sent a team to investigate and arrested Li Changmin, who was ringing the gong. The rest scattered. The county government also sent Wang Yibiao, a clerk from the first section, to survey the damage. Today (the 22nd), Li Changmin has been escorted to the county for interrogation.

Adulterer Strangles Husband to Death, Arrested and Brought to Justice: Wang Wentian of Tongjiaying in this county was strangled to death by his wife, Li, and her adulterer, Wang Wenxiang. Yesterday, Guo Wenhua, the director of the Banhu branch, arrested the adulterer Wang Wenxiang and brought him to justice. He was escorted to the county for interrogation today.

Pinghu 88

Water Police Capture Notorious Robber: Wang Shengcheng, the captain of the second squad of the ninth water police team, captured Qiao Laosan, a well-known lake bandit involved in the gun robbery case in Wuzhen, in Yuxian Dai the other day. Many stolen goods were seized on the spot. On the 19th, he was escorted to Pinghu for interrogation by Captain Hu. Qiao Laosan was not afraid at all and had a tough attitude. He confessed that he was 22 years old, from Suqian County, and that the bandit leader was currently in the Wujiang area. He also said that there were more than 600 bandits who robbed Wuzhen, traveling in 16 boats, and that each person was allocated 40 to 80 yuan, etc. The team escorted him to Hangzhou the other day for disposal. Yaqian Attacked by Bandits Again: At about 10:00 p.m. on the 23rd, 50 or 60 bandits suddenly came to Yaqian Town in the eastern countryside, carrying quick-firing guns and wooden-cased guns. They swarmed into the Xixie Yixing Store opened by Yao Youquan in the town and looted wantonly, and the losses are unknown. Then they went to Zhang Yihe's rice shop and burned all its account books. After the shooting, they marched east in formation. That night, three families, including the Zhou family, in the nearby countryside were also robbed by bandits.

Hangzhou 89

Debt Management Committee to Be Established on Schedule: The Zhejiang Provincial Construction Public Debt Fund Management Committee, with Wang Zuyao recommended by the General Chamber of Commerce, Jin Baishun recommended by the Banking Association, and Wang Ziqiu recommended by the Money Industry Association, will be established on March 1 in conjunction with the committee members appointed by the Provincial Government.

Security Team Strictly Guards the Zhejiang-Jiangxi Border: Jiangshan and Changshan counties on the Zhejiang-Jiangxi border have sent urgent telegrams to the Provincial Government, stating that the Jiangxi bandits have captured Shangrao and are about to invade Zhejiang. At the same time, they have telegraphed the first security regiment for troops. It is said that the regiment has dispatched troops to defend against them.

Hangping Highway to Be Open to Traffic Soon: The Zhejiang Provincial Highway Bureau has announced that the Hangping Highway project has been completed and that the opening ceremony will be held on March 23 and officially open to traffic on April 1.

Taiwan Tea Tax to Be Contracted Out: The Department of Finance has announced that Xu Wendao's contract for the Taiwan tea tax has expired and has stipulated that the minimum quota for the whole year is 12,000 yuan for both principal and supplementary taxes, and the contract period is one year, from 9:00 a.m. to 12:00 p.m. on March 8, and bids will be submitted to the Department.

Shangyu 90

Refugees Steal Items and Are Escorted Out of the Territory: A large number of refugees arrived in Gongjiafan in the western countryside on the afternoon of the 22nd, and divided into teams to beg for money and rice from various residences. In the home of the wealthy Yin Hu Gong Xingpu, more than ten male and female refugees suddenly broke in. At that time, Xingpu was lying in bed due to illness. First, six men surrounded the bed and begged for help. At the same time, six or seven female refugees slipped into the kitchen and asked Xingpu's two daughters-in-law to provide relief. The two daughters-in-law each agreed to give three silver yuan and solicit donations from the neighbors for assistance. Amidst the commotion, three or four companions came in and said that the villagers had given them 18 silver yuan and some food. They then called the female refugees out and left the village in formation. Xingpu's eldest daughter-in-law (wife of Zhao Lin) suspected that the female refugees' disregard for the promised silver was suspicious, so she went upstairs to search the boxes and cabinets. Unexpectedly, nine gold rings, one gold hairpin, one gold pick, one gold lock, and one pair of gold bracelets (weighing more than 30 taels in total) hidden in the clothes were all gone, leaving only a pearl butterfly that had not been stolen. She then sent someone to follow the refugees to find their residence, and reported the theft to the county government for recovery of the stolen goods. The county government, based on the situation, immediately ordered the county defense team and many police officers from the Public Security Bureau to go to the Dongyue Temple, three miles away from the city, and take the refugee leaders Wang Zhaolin, Wang Jindong, Wang Yongqing, and five others to the county. They were interrogated in court on the morning of the 23rd. They claimed to be from Huangmei County, Hubei, and arrived in Shangyu from Ningbo via Shaoxing on the 21st, and did not admit to any theft. However, after examining the passports, it was found that there were as many as 214 people registered, but only 134 people remained after checking. After repeated questioning, they firmly refused to confess. An order was issued to escort them and wait for instructions from the province. As for the hundred and several dozen refugees living in the Dongyue Temple, four fast boats from Fenghu, Mazhu, and Lianghu were sealed off on the morning of the 24th and ordered to leave the territory. The refugee side proposed conditions that they would not leave Shangyu unless the county released the five people who had been arrested. Finally, the county government presented the five refugee representatives, including Wang Zhaolin, who were detained, added instruments of torture, and prepared a document to be sent to the Yuyao County Government for transfer to the Ningbo Local Court for legal handling. The remaining refugees were escorted onto the ship by a large team of soldiers and police and also went to Yuyao.

Xiaoshan 91

He Shang Da San Xiang Requests Continued Relief Funds: The He Shang Da San Xiang in the southern countryside of Xiaoshan suffered particularly severe disaster last year, and wailing was heard everywhere. The county government has previously provided relief, but the amount of porridge was small and the monks were many, making it difficult to sustain. The village chiefs' joint meeting decided to recommend Zhang Songlou, Wei Ao, and others as representatives to go to the county to petition for continued relief funds. It is said that there are currently more than 7,600 disaster victims in the three townships, which is really not enough to distribute the relief funds.

Scheduled County-Wide Sports Meeting: The Xiaoshan County-wide Sports Meeting held a preparatory meeting on the 22nd and decided to hold it on March 16. The vice-chairman has left Xiaoshan, and Chuan Yun has been hired as the replacement.

Hefei 92

Sanhe Merchant Corps Repels Lake Bandits: The Sanhe Town Merchant Corps of Feinan, consisting of more than 30 members, escorted more than 200,000 yuan of cash to Wuwei and hired civilian boats. On the 20th, when passing through the southern part of Chaohu Lake on their way back, they were suddenly surrounded by three bandit boats full of bandits who shouted to surrender their weapons. A certain captain of the Merchant Corps immediately fired a pistol, shooting a bandit in black clothes into the lake. The bandits then fired their guns in unison, and the Merchant Corps also resisted as a whole, firing with machine guns. The bandits gradually became unable to withstand the attack. Just then, the Chaohu Water Police heard the sound and sent two patrol boats to assist. The battle lasted until dusk, and the bandit boats fled into the darkness. Two members of the Merchant Corps were shot in the legs and were taken to the city for treatment.

Joint Suppression of Bandits by Hefei and Lu'an Counties: The bandit atmosphere is rampant in the area where Ma Ji, Taiping Ji, Jin Qiao, and Guanting intersect between Hefei and Lu'an counties. Travelers are hesitant to travel, and transportation is cut off. County Magistrate Wang telegraphed County Magistrate Gao of Lu'an yesterday, scheduling to personally lead the team to suppress the bandits on the 25th. Lu'an was also requested to send a team to block and suppress the bandits in the Jin Qiao area in order to eliminate them in one fell swoop.

Talk on Education Programs (4) 94

The Education Program Compilation Committee of the Ministry of Education held a standing committee meeting at the Ministry of Education from 9:00 AM to 6:00 PM on the 25th. Committee members Yu Ziyi and Tao Xuan, as well as the Vice Minister, Directors, and Counselors of the Ministry of Education, were present. They first discussed the social education program (the most important part of this program is mass education, such as citizen literacy training, which has been incorporated into the adult remedial education plan), and a general decision was made: (1) to determine the goals and implementation methods of social education; (2) to plan vocational remedial education for farmers, workers, and merchants, as well as domestic affairs education; (3) to promote and reward art education methods; (4) to draft education methods for national independence movements from the perspective of social education; (5) to stipulate matters related to social education and school education (such as social education institutions attached to rural primary schools, etc.). The above items will be implemented separately within six years, with varying degrees of urgency. Also, (1) to promote public sports and implement the physical education law promulgated by the National Government; (2) to plan for the improvement of social customs and public entertainment (such as improving opera, drum storytelling, shadow plays, establishing model theaters, public tea rooms, etc., and methods for supervising and guiding social education institutions established by public and private organizations), which are planned to be implemented within one or two years. Also, (1) to plan for the establishment of central and provincial music halls, etc.; (2) to plan for the establishment of central and the promotion of provincial libraries, and to compile popular reading materials and various popular publications, which are planned to be implemented within three or four years. Also, (1) to plan for the establishment of central and provincial museums, and to formulate matters for the preservation of documents and antiquities; (2) to plan for special education for the mentally and physically disabled, and the rehabilitation education of criminals, which are planned to be implemented within five or six years. Although these were the opinions discussed at the time, it was generally agreed that the popularization of social education within six years should depend on economic capacity, and it should be carried out either in stages or simultaneously. Around 2:00 PM, because the full text of the social education program was very long, Director Chen presented the main points, and after discussion, a general decision was made. As for the content of the program, Vice Minister Liu will later designate a committee to slightly revise the wording, and it will be considered finalized. Then, the Mongolian and Tibetan education program was discussed. Counselor Wu Meixuan of the Mongolian and Tibetan Affairs Commission (who is the director of the Mongolian and Tibetan group of the program committee) attended and reported the main points of the Mongolian and Tibetan education program. Then, a detailed discussion was held on the brought program, such as the higher education and general education programs for Mongolia and Tibet, and solutions were discussed for each. The most important thing is to plan to establish three middle schools, normal schools, and vocational schools within six years as a step towards promoting Mongolian and Tibetan education. The discussion continued late into the night. Regarding the Mongolian and Tibetan education program, except for the two items of educational administration and social education, which Counselor Wu will continue to send to the Ministry for review and signing by the committee members, the rest were passed. The Ministry of Education has been holding program meetings for days, and the Vice Minister, Directors, Counselors, etc., have been holding meetings during the day and reviewing official documents at night, which is extremely busy. At this point, the program meeting came to a brief conclusion, and normal work was resumed.
