Inheritance Dispute After the Death of Fang Danchi 144

Many Gold Leaves and Gold Pounds Involved

Both Sides Sue Each Other in Three Cases

The Three Cases Have Progressed One After Another

Fang Danchi, a close relative of Fang Benren, passed away in Shanghai last autumn. The movable property he left behind is estimated to be worth about 200,000 gold. In addition, there were gold leaves and gold pounds, worth more than 4,000 yuan, which had disappeared without a trace. Later, Danchi's son, Dacheng, found that his father's concubine, Deng, and servant, Wang Dahan, had stolen them and handed them over to Deng Guannan, his father's friend, who in turn gave them to Wang Shutang for joint embezzlement. He demanded their return, but they refused. Later, because he had to escort the coffin back to his hometown, he had no time to continue the investigation. Until last December, Deng Guannan suddenly came to Shanghai from Hankou. Dacheng feared that he had come to Shanghai to withdraw money from the bank, so he followed him. Before long, Deng's daughter also came to Shanghai from Hankou. Dacheng then hired lawyer Zhan Jifeng to sue Deng and his daughter, as well as the two Wangs, in the Provisional Court for stealing the inheritance. To prevent Deng Guannan from escaping, he lived in the same Hongkou Hotel as Deng. Unexpectedly, Deng reported to the Hongkou police that Fang Dacheng had engaged in kidnapping. The detective chief sent detectives to arrest Fang. After explaining the situation, he was detained for several hours for no reason. Therefore, Fang also entrusted his agent lawyer Zhan Jifeng to further accuse Deng and his daughter of fabricating false accusations. Deng Guannan also, through his agent lawyer, filed a lawsuit accusing Fang Dacheng and Fang's fifth uncle, Fang Fengchi, as well as Hu Hanqing, Zhou Shanbang, and others, of illegal detention and obstructing freedom. The case has already been heard once.

Fang Dacheng's Lawsuit for Theft 145

Unable to Enter the Sickroom Frequently Yesterday afternoon, the scheduled hearing continued. The defendant, Wang Shutang, surrendered himself to the police and hired lawyer Jiang Yiping to defend him. Wang Dahan, Hu Hanqing, and Zhou Shanbang, the other defendants, did not appear. Soon, Judge Luo Renji ascended to the 14th Court and announced that the three lawsuits filed by both parties should be heard, starting with Fang Dacheng's lawsuit for theft. According to the plaintiff, Fang Dacheng, after my father fell ill, Deng Jin alienated the relationship between my father and son, so I was unable to enter the sickroom frequently. Only Deng and Wang Dahan were at my father's side.

Stealing Gold Pounds and Gold Leaves From July 21 to August 3 last year, when my father was critically ill, they stole the gold pounds and gold leaves in the iron box and all the passbooks and vouchers in the leather bag. Deng took the gold items to the room of her father, Deng Guannan, downstairs, and Guannan took them to Bao Lingfeng's house and gave them to Wang Shutang to take away.

More Than 300,000 Gold During His Lifetime Fang Fengchi testified that when my brother passed away, I received a letter in Hankou and arrived in Shanghai on August 6. There are seven brothers in my family, and we have not yet divided the family property, which is jointly owned and managed by Danchi. The various current and fixed deposits amounted to about 200,000 yuan, and the real estate was no less than 300,000 yuan.

Only a Few Hundred Gold After His Death After Danchi's death, there were only four deposit books with deposits of only three or four hundred yuan. The rest was gone. When Danchi was ill, Deng and Wang Dahan handled most of the withdrawals.

It Is Difficult to Investigate the Deposits When I arrived in Shanghai, I learned that there was no cash at home, and funds were needed for the funeral. I planned to take the gold pounds and gold leaves, so I opened the iron box, but they were gone. I asked Deng, who said she had taken them. I also had Wang Shutang mortgage the tobacco leaf bill of lading. I also investigated the deposits, but my brother usually stored them under other names, so it was difficult to investigate, and so on.

Keeping Gold Pounds and Gold Leaves Also, Bao Zhenpeng, the nephew of the witness Bao Lingfeng, testified that Wang Shutang came to my house at 1:00 PM on August 5 last year, and then Deng Guannan also came and gave the gold items to Wang, asking him to keep them. After inspection, there were 80 gold pounds and a package of gold leaves, about 10 taels. This is what I saw, and there was nothing else, and so on.

Mortgaging Gold Pounds to a Coffin Shop When asked, the defendant Wang Shutang confessed that he was a friend of Danchi. On the day of his death, his family asked me to buy clothes and a coffin for him. The next day, Deng took 88 gold pounds and gold leaves to Bao's house and asked me to keep them. On the 11th of this month, because the 455 yuan for the coffin had not been paid, I temporarily mortgaged the gold pounds to the Jufeng Wood Shop at the Xin Matou in Nanshi, which sold the coffin. On the 12th, the funds from the tobacco leaf mortgage were made, and I took back the gold pounds and returned them to Deng and his daughter. The gold leaves were also returned. I do not know whether the gold items were given to Deng by Danchi or taken privately by Liu Deng.

The Gold Pounds Can Be Investigated Lawyer Zhan immediately presented various documents, bills, and coffin purchase invoices to prove that Wang Shutang's confession could not be believed, and said that the gold pounds and gold leaves were not temporarily mortgaged to Jufeng. This can be investigated, and so on.

My Husband Gave Me the Gold Pounds Deng also confessed that the gold items were given to her by her husband in May or June last year because she had sold her gold jewelry before and she had argued with him, so he gave her the gold pounds, etc. When her husband passed away, her sixth uncle, Hechi, wanted to claim the gold items, and Dacheng even wanted to search for them, so she and her father sent them to Bao's house and asked Wang to keep them. Later, Wang returned the original items. Deng Guannan's confession about the gold items was roughly the same as his daughter's.

A Card Written in His Own Hand While Ill Fang Fengchi believed that Deng and others' statements that his brother had sold the lady's jewelry were completely inaccurate. He presented evidence to prove that his family had a lot of current deposits at that time, and his brother would never have sold the jewelry. He also presented a card, saying that the card was written in Danchi's own hand while ill, listing the amount of deposits in various places, totaling more than 60,000 gold. He also said that Deng had previously confessed to 36 gold pounds, but now she said 80 gold pounds. He requested an investigation to determine the exact number.

Fang Dacheng's Lawsuit Accusing Deng and His Daughter of False Accusation 146

The Father and Daughter Accuse Me of Kidnapping In the second hearing of Fang Dacheng's lawsuit accusing Deng and his daughter of false accusation, Fang stated that on February 7, Deng reported to the Hongkou police that he had kidnapped her, which resulted in Chinese and Western detectives coming to arrest him and inflict torture on him. He was first detained at the Hongkou police station and then escorted to the Huisi police station. After I explained the situation, I was released. Before reporting to the police, Deng had gone to the Hongkou Hotel to meet with her father, so it was actually a conspiracy between the father and daughter.

Police Detectives Testify A detective from the Hongkou police station, No. 17, testified that Deng and her representative lawyer went to the police station to report, and I asked the lawyer, who said that the accusation was illegal detention, so I went to arrest Fang. I did not hear the word kidnapping at the time.

The Question of Reporting to the Police and Kidnapping When asked, Deng confessed that she reported to the police that Dacheng had illegally detained my father, and I had never discussed it with my father beforehand. Deng Guannan said that my daughter came to Shanghai because I summoned her in a letter, but I did not know about her reporting to the police at first. At that time, lawyer Zhan said that Deng had indeed mentioned kidnapping when reporting to the police. Please investigate the records of the police station. The court approved it.

Deng Guannan's Lawsuit for Obstructing Freedom 147

Monitoring His Actions After Arriving in Shanghai In the final hearing of Deng Guannan's lawsuit for obstructing freedom, Deng stated that after arriving in Shanghai, Fang's uncle and nephew, as well as Hu Hanqing and Zhou Shanbang, searched his luggage, took away his travel expenses, and monitored his actions. The two parties denied all of his accusations and responded to each accusation.

The hearing had lasted for six hours. Judge Luo ordered the defendants to continue to be released on bail by their lawyers and adjourned the hearing to March 5.

It was not me who drove at the time, and so on. Chief Judge Zhou verified the confession and ordered the defendants to be remanded in custody separately and adjourned the retrial to a later date.

Yao Yinfo and His Wife Receive Extortion Letters Together 149

Detectives Negotiate on the Phone

All Extortion Letters Are Delivered by the Bandits Themselves

How Do the Bandits Know Song Shuying?

Her Cousin Is Involved

Yao Yinfo, a native of Huzhou, residing at No. 208 Chunhua Lane, Meibaige Road, is a clerk at Zhu Sifu's law firm. He has been married to Ms. Song Shuying for more than ten years. Since the 19th of this month, he has received a series of letters from bandits, a total of five, some addressed to Yao and some to Song, and the content is all about demanding 1,000 yuan. Yao then sent the letters to the Xin Zha Police Station, which had jurisdiction over the area, and asked them to investigate. Because the letters he received were all sent to the door by bandits and thrown through the door slits, he expected them to continue to do so. Therefore, the police chief sent detectives Zhou Guisheng and Ma Zhonglai to Yao's house on the 24th of this month to station there. That afternoon, the telephone at Yao's house rang loudly. Detective Ma picked up the phone. At first, he heard the other party asking if the person on the phone was Song Shuying. Ma said yes. He also asked if the previous letter had been received. Ma knew that it was the bandit on the phone, so he replied that it had been read. Then, he began to negotiate. Ma told him that the family was not wealthy and could only afford three or four hundred gold, otherwise it would be difficult to raise the money. The person on the other end said that if they were sincere in negotiating, they could put a red paper with the amount written on it on the door of their house, and there would be a letter the next day to arrange a meeting place. After saying this, the phone rang again, and the conversation ended. Ma ordered Yao's family to do as agreed and reported back to the police station. On the 25th (the day before), at 8:00 AM, Ma went to Yao's house again and learned that the bandit had thrown a letter there, which stated that they would talk again in the afternoon, and so on. Waiting until 6:30 PM, another letter was thrown through the door slit of Yao's house. Ma immediately opened the door and saw one

person running away. He chased after him. Detective Zhou Guisheng and Detective Zong Weiting also arrived to assist in the chase. The person fled to Taiping Lane and went straight into the house at No. 10. He was chased and captured by Chinese patrol officer No. 127 of the Third Squad and Western patrol officer No. 242 and taken to the police station. He confessed his name as Xu Er, a native of Shanghai, and was taken into custody. It was then learned that Xu did not know Yao's address at first, so his initial extortion letters were mistakenly thrown into the house of Zhao Xu, a woman at No. 209 Qingdao Road. The woman's family was poor and knew that they were not qualified to be scammed, so she ignored it. Later, because she received three consecutive letters, she had to take the letters to the police station to report them. Ma and others verified that the handwriting was the same as that on the letters received by Yao, and the names were also the same. Therefore, it was suspected that the bandit had thrown them by mistake. Yesterday morning, Xu and the letters were escorted to the Provisional Court. Judge Luo Renji conducted a preliminary hearing. After the police lawyer, Ru Baoyi, presented the case, he requested an adjournment. Then, Yao Yinfo and his wife came to court to testify about what had happened. Yao also said that his wife's name was Song Shuying, which few outsiders knew. How the bandit knew it was difficult to figure out, and so on. When asked, Xu Er confessed that I was studying at a certain school. This matter was initiated by a cousin of Song Shuying, and I wrote the letters and delivered them four times on his behalf. Judge Luo ordered the defendant to be held in custody and adjourned the hearing to a later date.

Li Zhaoquan Sentenced to Seven Years

Li Jingnan Sentenced to Nine Years for Two Crimes

After the robbery at the home of Li Zhaobing, a Cantonese native at No. 2017 North Sichuan Road, Feng Qi, a detective from the Hongkou police station, arrested the victim's nephew, Li Zhaoquan, and the Cantonese natives Li Jingnan and Xu Er, and escorted them to the Provisional Court for investigation, as reported in the previous newspaper. According to the investigation by Detective Feng and Deputy Western Detective Bailisi, Li Zhaoquan was only involved in this case, while Li Jingnan was also involved in the armed robbery of a certain family at No. 768 Wuchang Road by a gang on November 20 of last year. The guns and ammunition were confiscated, and the stolen goods were returned to the original owner. Xu Er was released because he was not involved.

He was in financial difficulties, and his wife's work was not enough to make a living, so she committed suicide. He had no money for a coffin and burial and would need to seek help from his fellow villagers. Upon hearing the report, Judge Ge instructed Wu to sign a pledge to claim the body for coffin and burial.

Swallowing Matches

Ma Guisheng, a 30-year-old Suzhou native residing at No. 32 Gaoshou Li, Haining Road, was employed at the Reiss & Co. on Rue de Ningpo. His wife, Wang, was 23 years old, also from Suzhou. The couple had a quarrel over trivial matters the previous morning. Ma then went to his office. After work, he saw his wife lying in bed. She did not eat that evening. Ma thought that family disputes were common, so he ignored it. They slept in the same bed that night. However, Ma woke up at midnight and heard his wife moaning and vomiting. Ma turned on the light and saw that his wife looked pale. When the landlord and others arrived after being alerted, they questioned her and learned that she had swallowed a box of matches. They hired a streetcar to take her to Baolong Hospital for treatment. However, the poison had penetrated deep into her organs, and treatment was ineffective. She died at around 5 a.m.

News of Printed Ci Poetry Score 157

"Ci Pu" (詞譜), in 40 volumes, was officially compiled in the 54th year of the Kangxi reign of the Qing Dynasty. It includes more than 820 tunes and 2,300 forms, arranged in order of the number of characters. The punctuation and rhyming are indicated in small characters below the words. The tones of each character, whether level or oblique, or whether level or oblique are allowed, are marked with symbols next to the characters. The origins of the names of various lyrics, the level and oblique tones of melodies, the differences in sentence structure, and the suites of large pieces are all researched extensively and authoritatively. This allows scholars to follow the rules and provides a comprehensive collection of Ci poetry. If we can use this to determine the rules of Ci poetry and discuss the musical modes, we may be able to obtain the lost musical chapters and restore the old music of Dasheng. Therefore, those who write Ci poetry today must follow the words and sentences determined by the score, distinguish their level and oblique tones, and further divide the level tones into those replaced by entering tones and those replaced by rising tones, and divide the oblique tones into those suitable for rising, falling, or entering tones. Only then can it be considered a complete Ci poetry that can be scored for musical instruments, harmonizing with jade flutes, red teeth, Qin zithers, and Yan reeds in singing and dancing venues. However, this book is rarely circulated and cannot be obtained for less than 200 yuan. Now there is a lithographic edition, priced at only 10 yuan per copy. If you want to view a sample, please send a letter to the Medical Bookstore at No. 121 Meibai Road, Shanghai.

"New Classic of Mountains and Seas" Novel Sells Well 158

The famous novelist Mr. Zhang Qiuchong has recently completed a novel called "New Classic of Mountains and Seas". The content is profound and the writing is fluent. The materials used are mostly interesting stories from the societies of Ping, Jin and Hu (Beijing, Tianjin and Shanghai). The vivid and lifelike depictions are endlessly readable. Each set of five books is packaged in a brocade box and priced at five yuan. It is sold by the Central Bookstore in Qingyunli, Maijiaquan, Shanghai. Sales have been very brisk recently. The first edition is almost sold out, and the second edition is being rushed into print.

On February 21, 1930, a strangled female corpse was found near the intersection of Huanyang Road and Tangshan Road. She was five feet two inches tall, about 15 to 20 years old, of medium build, with black hair and pale yellow skin, brown eyes, a short and flat nose, a round face, flat ears, and a high forehead. She was wearing a red vest, a black and white striped cloth vest, and a white cloth small vest, blue pants, white socks, and black shoes. Achievements of the Hongqiao Qingpu Nursery 164

West of the Hongqiao Airport in this port is the Qingpu Nursery, which was founded by a private individual. It has more than 400 mu of land and has planted more than one million trees. The tallest trees are already fifteen or sixteen feet tall and three inches in diameter. Since last autumn, it has been distributing seedlings to various highways and gardens. After learning about this, the government's afforestation agencies have been purchasing from it one after another. The nursery has also contributed a part of its strength in donations. Recently, Mr. Fan Dianxia, the manager of the nursery, was invited to Beijing and the provincial capital, and received high praise from the Agricultural Committee of the Ministry of Agriculture, the Provincial Department of Agriculture, and the Provincial Governor of Civil Affairs, Mr. Miao. It is hoped that private individuals can continue to do so.

The Xujiahui Observatory predicted at 4:30 p.m. yesterday that the sky would be cloudy and slightly cold. There was fog in the Yangtze River basin and rain off the coast south of Maanshan Island. Strong seasonal winds from the northwest to the northeast prevailed along the coast of the entire country. The weather in western Japan was bad. Also, within 24 hours before 3 p.m. yesterday, the highest temperature in this port was 57.4 degrees and the lowest was 51.8 degrees. Free Talk

A Word of Wisdom 174

— Xu Xiaoting

If your lover gets angry, don't talk to them. Because when you talk at this time, the feelings of both parties are most likely to break down.

Women's love of beauty is more intense than that of men. In fact, men's love of beauty even surpasses that of women.

The most terrifying woman on the stage of love is a woman who embraces romanticism. Because they most like to play with men.

Although divorce is agreed upon by both husband and wife, in fact, in one hundred divorce cases, there are several cases where the husband or wife is passive.

People who value reputation and morality cannot experience life in prison.

Only when the body becomes frail does one realize the joy of a strong and healthy time.

In court cases involving human life, apart from theft and robbery, most are cases of adultery between men and women. This shows the harm of lust.

Discovery of Hidden Gold in Huzhou 175

— Yu Xiao

The discovery of hidden gold is often seen in newspapers. Most of them are untrue or incomplete. What I am recording now is particularly credible and substantiated. The person speaking is an eyewitness. The event is not far from today. It happened on Clothing Street in Huzhou. Initially, since the beginning of the Political Tutelage, all major cities have been engaged in municipal construction. Huzhou is no exception. It specially renovated the streets inside and outside the city, and uniformly widened them to facilitate pedestrians. As a result, nine out of ten shops and residences on the street had to be demolished and moved back a few feet. There were hundreds of road construction workers. The sounds of shovels were loud. This work was praised by some and complained about by others. This is a major local policy, which is unrelated to this topic, so I won't say too much. I should record the unusual discovery of hidden gold. There was a cloth shop called Zhengfeng on Clothing Street. Its storefront was also in the demolition zone. On the original site of the Zhengfeng shop, a worker dug down with a hoe. Suddenly, he hit a hard object. Upon inspection, it was a mud ball. Removing the dirt, it revealed a glittering golden color. It was a Yuanbao! He couldn't help but be overjoyed. Other workers all gathered upon hearing the sound. They passed it around and looked at it. It was indeed a pure gold Yuanbao. They thought there must be more than one. They dug further at the spot. They successively dug up sixteen silver ones and twelve gold ones. Each weighed several dozen taels. They were all engraved with the words "Yuanfeng." It is unknown what year they were lost. The workers suddenly acquired this unexpected windfall. They all thought of taking possession. They kept fighting each other. It almost led to disaster. Fortunately, there was a Lu Zhonglian who came out to mediate. He distributed them according to their names. Only then did they happily share the loot and finish the matter. The discovery of hidden gold seems strange but is not surprising. It must have been buried by someone first, and then discovered by someone later. It is not creating something from nothing. Only superstitious people might regard it as a gift from the God of Wealth. As a result, they become even more flattering to the gods. They think hard and try their best, hoping to gain something. In fact, in history, there have been many rebellions. Rich families often buried their wealth before fleeing from disaster. It is truly a case of "no place is without treasure." The opportunity to discover it is also something that can only be encountered and not sought. After the discovery of gold and silver Yuanbao on Clothing Street in Huzhou, workers constructing roads on other streets at the same time suddenly had delusions. Therefore, I explain it by analogy.

Travel Tips 176

— Meng Qi

As the saying goes, "It's good to be at home for a thousand days, but it's hard to go out for even a moment." Indeed, going out is not an easy thing. The following is something I personally experienced. Writing it down may serve as a warning to those who have not yet been deceived.

When the Yangtze River steamer arrived in Shanghai, we were busy disembarking. Because there were several people traveling together, we agreed to put our luggage together. When we arrived at the pier, a tout from a certain inn suddenly rushed in. Without asking for permission, he grabbed our belongings and ran away. He gave us a copper tag, saying that we could use this tag to retrieve our belongings at the inn. Since our belongings had already been taken away, there was no way to stop him. We had no choice but to listen to him. He then called a carriage for us and took us to the inn.

We had to let him do as he pleased in order to get our belongings back. When we arrived at the inn, we saw that there were quite a few fellow sufferers. We knew that this would be a big rip-off. One person who brought two items was charged twelve yuan. Later, it was settled for five yuan. We saw that things were not good. It wasn't just about paying money, but our belongings were slow to arrive. We were as anxious as ants in a hot pot. But since we were already at their mercy, we had no choice but to let them slaughter us. Later, a friend felt that this was outrageous. He secretly went out and called two patrol officers. The patrol officers asked about everything in detail and greatly reduced the price. When the inn saw the patrol officers, they panicked. The belongings were brought over, and the price they asked for was lower. However, they kept cursing under their breath. They almost became violent. In the end, we paid five yuan before we could escape from the tiger's mouth.

Therefore, I feel that anyone arriving in Shanghai by Yangtze River steamer should never open the door upon arrival. Once the door is opened, problems will arise. It's best to wait a while and let the crowd disperse before going out leisurely. Otherwise, you'll end up paying unfairly and being laughed at.

A Visit to the Spring Gathering of the Xiling Painting and Calligraphy Society 177

— Wang Meiqu From Hangzhou

Painting and calligraphy are the quintessence of our country. Since the eastward spread of European styles, writing has imitated crab-walking, and painting has focused on watercolors and pencil oil painting. The old models of seal, clerical, running, and regular script, as well as realistic color painting, have almost disappeared. Hangzhou has an organization called the Xiling Painting and Calligraphy Society. My daughter, Yunhua, has recently been forced by circumstances to temporarily live with her mother. In her spare time from raising children, she was ordered by her mother to study painting and calligraphy with a teacher. In the past six months, her works in seal script, figure painting, flowers, etc., have been quite decent. She was admitted to the society as a member. February 16th was the date of the seventh spring gathering of the society. Two days earlier, I received an invitation from two elders of the society, Mr. Wang Qianlou and Mr. Lu Aitang, inviting my wife and me to visit. My wife was just recovering from an illness and could not be exposed to the wind. I went alone to visit and recorded what I saw below.

The Society's History and Address: The Society has been carefully organized by Hangzhou's elders and celebrities for seven years. The society's address is temporarily located at No. 19 Zhijian Road Lane. During the visit, Mr. Shen Shijia, a member of the society, told me that the society displays the works of its members once every spring. Fortunately, the number of members is increasing day by day. The leaders of the society are actively seeking to expand its development. Even the address of the society is being considered for relocation to a better place.

The Grand Occasion of the Gathering on That Day: The gathering opened at 9:00 AM and ended at 4:00 PM with a dinner and photo session. More than 140 male and female members of the society attended, with more than 60 people present. Because the society's exhibition space was a bit narrow, each member's calligraphy and paintings could not be hung up individually. However, those who collaborated on painting and calligraphy on the spot, such as Wang Qianlou, Lu Aitang, Shen Shijia, Zhu Jinglu, Hu Yaguang, Wu Jianhua, and female members He Huanwei, Fan Shichang, Fang Shuqing, Chuan Leiqing, and others, were proficient in the four styles of calligraphy and followed the former sages in painting. They were all modest at first when they waved their brushes to the guests. When they showed their skills, each was truly unwilling to yield. My daughter, Yunhua, also followed suit, bringing her standing scroll of seal script and meticulous painting of "Seven Sons." She was praised by the teachers and friends in the society. The visitors also had no derogatory words. She also completed the second half of the "Willow Shoots and Green Clouds" poem written by Shen Shijia in collaboration with Meixi Landscape under the teacher's order. All the ladies also had works that were worthy of being recited and read.

The Joyful Gathering at the Dinner: On this day, male and female members of the society and guests gathered in one hall. They were seated in the spacious house of a society member and toasted each other in separate seats. Male and female guests and members of the society were seated separately. The guests praised. Qianlou, Aitang, and Shijia all responded with humble words. Aitang once had a day of elegance, and he admired articles on political affairs. I revered Qianlou for the first time, and he abandoned his glory and indulged in painting and calligraphy, especially landscapes. Shijia is a young and promising talent who enters and exits between Mi Dian and Mo Jie. The calligraphy of Miss Chuan Leiqing and the Western paintings of Mr. Hu Yaguang are also not easy to come by. All members of the association are impeccable. My daughter is fortunate to follow the refined arts.

Letter to the Editor: I recently read a news item in your publication about Hangzhou City, which stated that a large tiger in Huangjiahu Village, Thirteen Du, Xixiang, Zhuji, near Jiguan Mountain, was captured by villagers Huang Baiyou and others while hunting in the mountains and transported to Hangzhou for sale. It was then purchased by Hu Qingyutang in Dajing Lane for 1,300 yuan, etc. After checking, I found that the facts were different and not true. I have lived in Dingqing Village, Zhuji County, for generations and have always relied on hunting for a living. On the ninth day of the first month of this year, according to the old calendar, I discovered the footprints of a large tiger at the foot of Tiandong Mountain, a distance from my village. After studying them, the tiger's body was incomparably large and unusually ferocious. It seemed that a few people could not capture it. So I invited fifteen colleagues to track and hunt it separately. We started on the eleventh day at dawn and captured it at risk. Later, it was transported to Hangzhou and sold to Yezhongde Tang Pharmacy on Wangxianqiao Straight Street, receiving a real price of 350 yuan in silver. We returned to the village and divided the profits equally among ourselves. Unexpectedly, yesterday, due to your newspaper's misreporting of the tiger's sale price as 1,300 yuan, due to the long distance and brief words, it led to a misunderstanding. My fellow hunters were all suspicious and questioned me, believing that the seller had forgotten the meaning of shared hardship in the face of profit, embezzling the price to enrich himself. Although I explained it in every possible way, it was still difficult to obtain the understanding of the parties concerned. However, I have always admired your newspaper for its realistic reporting and emphasis on actual events. I am writing this special letter to explain the details, hoping that you will quickly correct the record to clarify the truth and avoid disputes. I am eternally grateful. With this letter, I salute you, Mr. Da Yi Bi. Your humble servants, Jiang Dingwen and Zhao Ating, together with Yin. February 21st.

Overseas News

Italy Orders Women's Clothing to Return to the Past 178

— Guo Xin

Rome, Italy, February 21st (Special Telegram): The headquarters of the Italian Fascist Party has announced the style of women's clothing for the coming year in Italy. Long skirts, narrow collars, and long sleeves that reach the hands are very similar to the ancient clothing of the fourteenth century. The colors will exclude bright and beautiful colors and focus on green and gray. From now on, Italian women's clothing will be completely unaffected by the new fashions of other countries.

Translator's note: The Fascist Party is the political party formed by the great modern politician, Italian Prime Minister, and dictator Mussolini.

[P Little Recipe

— Yang Yixiao

Dregs Mutton Cut the Hu mutton into pieces. Add aged dregs soup, bean curd skin, and spring bamboo shoots. Put them in a clay pot and simmer them on a charcoal stove. It is fresh and delicious.

Crab Paste Skin Take lice crabs and crush them in a stone mortar. Filter out their shells. Then mix them with duck eggs. Use a piece of raw lard and spread it on a hot wok. Its taste is extremely delicious.

Stewed Pickled Fresh Cut pickled fresh meat into square pieces. Add spring bamboo shoots and bean curd skin knots. Place them in a casserole and simmer them over low heat.

It is exceptionally rich and delicious.

New Sounds of Peking Opera 179

— Liu Henwo From Beiping

Since the Spring Festival, one of the changes in the Peking Opera circle in Pingzhong is the implementation of co-starring by men and women. The audience attendance is very good. Therefore, all the famous actors have invited female actors to cooperate. For example, Yang Xiaolou and Yan Jupeng are co-starring with Xin Qiuzhi at the Kaiming Theater. Hao Shuchen and Wu Tiean are co-starring with Zhang Guoyun at the Hualeyuan. Yu Sheng Sun, who has not dedicated himself to the red velvet for a long time, is also performing with He Shunqin at the Sanqingyuan. Ma Lianliang, who returned to Ping from Shanghai, also plans to invite Du Liyun. Shang Xiaoyun has also changed course and is looking for a female actor to perform.

Since the classes have set a precedent for co-starring by men and women, the Jixiangyuan in Dong'an Market in the city was the first to break the new record of separating men and women. According to the old customs in Pingzhong, men were on the left and women were on the right, and they were never mixed up. Now, it has been approved to have men and women sit together, which is very popular. Therefore, the Jixiangyuan is full day and night.

One evening after the lanterns were lit, Yang Xiaolou's "An Tian Hui" and Yan Jupeng's and Xin Yanqiu's "Visiting Mother and Returning Home" at the Kaiming Theater were extremely crowded. The theater was full at 8 o'clock. However, Xin Yanqiu forgot his command arrow when he was leading the order on stage. Then, he turned around and shouted for the inspector. He was severely heckled by the entire audience. It is said that Xin Yanqiu sobbed incessantly after leaving the stage. The critics in Pingzhong are often demanding. In fact, a small flaw is not a big deal. The critics are unaware, but the recipients are embarrassed. It is not easy to sell art on the singing stage.

Xue Yanqin is the most popular female actor among the kun actors. She often visits the boudoirs of noble families. She has been performing at Jixiang continuously for days. Female customers account for six out of ten of the audience. Yesterday, the seventh concubine of a certain director specially requested a performance of "Flower Field Wrong." She reserved more than a dozen boxes and invited all her sisters. Xue Yanqin's magic is not weak.

Eastward Travel Correspondence (1) 180

— Wu Xiaohou

I have been involved in the spheres of national self-governance and social education for over a decade. This year, in August, I embarked on a journey. The purpose of this trip is solely to investigate the municipal administration and social education of major Japanese cities. However, as I am also one of the supervisors of the Jiangsu Provincial Newspaper Association and have been commissioned by Mr. Shi Liangcai, the manager of this newspaper, to serve as a special correspondent stationed in Japan, I will not only visit Japanese municipal administration and social education institutions but also report on newspapers, schools, historical scenic spots, and other places. For the sake of systematic and organized reporting, I will use my personal observations from visiting Nagasaki, Tokyo, Yokohama, Nagoya, Kyoto, Osaka, and Kobe as the framework. This will include the municipal administration and social education institutions of these major cities. I will also cover newspapers, schools, historical scenic spots, and other places, recording them in chronological order of my visits. This will provide a clear and organized overview. I hope to use the experiences of others to provide insights for our country. I hope that the readers find it interesting.

(1) Retrospective before the journey

I have been involved in the spheres of national self-governance and social education for over a decade. In the autumn of the eleventh year of the Republic [1922], I was specially dispatched by the Jiangsu Provincial Government to Shanxi to investigate self-governance administration. During my two-month stay in Shanxi, I traveled through three prefectures and eleven counties. Upon my return, I compiled my observations into "A True Record of Self-Governance Administration in Shanxi," which was published and circulated in multiple editions. I have never dared to be complacent. I had long planned to travel abroad to investigate municipal administration, hoping to gather diverse perspectives. Originally, I intended to travel to Europe and America. However, due to the high cost of traveling west, it was difficult to raise the funds in a short time. Later, I met Mr. Shi Liangcai, the manager of this newspaper, who suggested that our eastern neighbor, Japan, had been emulating Europe and America for many years. By striving continuously, they had achieved great things. Why not go there first to observe and learn? The journey would be shorter and less expensive, making it easier to realize. Therefore, I prepared everything and resolved to travel east. I was grateful to Zhao, the former minister of the Ministry of Interior, for providing a letter of introduction, and to Zhou, the director of the Asian Department of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, for writing a letter to our ambassador to Japan, Wang Gunfu, to assist me in everything. In August, I took the Shanghai Maru eastward. Accompanying me were Ms. Du Huairong, a graduate of the former Shanghai Xinhua Art University, and Mr. Mao Qiubai, a Bachelor of Arts from the Imperial University of Japan. The Shanghai Maru was scheduled to set sail at 9:00 AM. I boarded at 7:00 AM. That day, I woke up at 5:00 AM and went to the wharf by car at 6:00 AM. There were very few visitors. With only a shoulder bag, I set off on a solitary journey. The sound of birds bid me farewell, and the color of the grass seemed to hold me back. As we set sail, a heavy rain suddenly came. The clouds and water were vast and misty. Fortunately, the small boat sailed without wind or waves. We arrived in Nagasaki at 12:00 PM the next morning. After anchoring, I learned that the ship would depart at 5:00 PM. The sea journey was tedious. With five hours to spare, time was precious. So, I accompanied Ms. Du to have lunch ashore and then visited Mr. Lin Zheqing, our consul in Nagasaki. He kindly asked Mr. Sun Lifu, the chief officer of the consulate, to accompany us to visit various municipal administration and social education institutions in Nagasaki. At 4:30 PM, I returned to the ship with Mr. Lin. Consul Lin came to the wharf to see us off. As we bid farewell, the ship's whistle sounded, and we set sail for Kobe.

(2) Investigation in Nagasaki

(A) Municipal Administration

Accompanied by Mr. Sun and Ms. Du from the Nagasaki consulate, I went to the Nagasaki City Hall (i.e., the Municipal Government). Mayor Tominaga was away on official business, so Deputy Mayor Tamaki Shogo received us. I learned that the mayors of Japanese cities are all elected by the people, and there is a city council to decide on matters within the city's scope. The councilors are also elected by the people. This is different from the current system in China's special and ordinary cities, where mayors are appointed administratively and there is no city council. However, under each city hall in Japan, there are also separate bureaus for education, civil engineering, social affairs, and finance, which are under the jurisdiction of the city and handle matters within their respective areas. This is generally the same as the bureaus under Chinese cities. Although the mayor is elected by the people, he is supervised by the prefectural governor in the prefecture and by the governor of the prefecture in the prefecture (Japan's administrative organization includes the two prefectures of Tokyo and Kyoto, and the forty-three prefectures of Nagasaki and Hyogo, etc. Each prefecture has a prefectural governor. Hokkaido and Karafuto each have a director. Taiwan, Korea, and Kwantung Leased Territory each have a governor-general. The South Pacific Islands are under the mandate of the League of Nations' Paris Peace Conference). This is different from the parallel relationship between cities and provinces or special cities and provinces in China. The city currently has 39,503 households and a population of 248,447. The annual income is 2,584,156 yen. The annual expenditure is 1,402,830 yen for regular expenses and 1,181,326 yen for temporary expenses, totaling the same amount as the annual income. The expenditure items include waterworks fees, harbor fees, housing fees, afforestation basic property, education funds, compatriot relief funds, town-owned funds, coal disaster compensation, city bond repayment accumulation funds, and public hall construction funds, totaling nine items. There are approximately 1,200 Chinese expatriates in the city, mostly engaged in commerce and industry, with a few monks. This place is close to China and is the first port of entry from China to Japan. It is also one of the country's strongholds. The city streets are clean, but there are few new buildings. Most of the houses are still old-fashioned Japanese low houses. Because Nagasaki is an ordinary city, it cannot be compared with the six major cities of Tokyo, Yokohama, Nagoya, Kyoto, Osaka, and Kobe.

Grain and River Rice Market Turns Stable 190

Zhabei Yesterday's arrivals tended to be scarce, sales remained sluggish. Northern japonica rice prices rose due to reports of high production costs in inland areas, and rumors of merchants from Changzhou and Wuxi actively buying, leading to upward pressure on market prices. However, this was inconsistent with Shanghai customs prices, and the Shanghai prices had been frequently lowered due to sluggish sales, resulting in reduced source supply. River-stored cargo merchants unanimously refrained from selling, so although central japonica rice prices were affected by sluggish sales, they were better than the previous day, with the downward trend largely stabilized. Transactions in thin-husked rice remained weak, and the market trended flat. There were a few customers inquiring about foreign indica rice, and the market was active, but prices did not fluctuate. Due to the low price of foreign rice, Du-bu indica rice showed no improvement in small-lot sales, and the overall market went from weak to stable. The various grades of "Lian Yin Yuan" rice saw gradually improving buying interest, and recent arrivals were not sufficient, leading to active liquidation at favorable prices. Overall, the volume of goods traded throughout the day remained low, with a total of less than 3,000 piculs.

South Shanghai River rice arrivals were being received, but street sales were not smooth. It was difficult to reduce prices for Changzhou and Northern japonica rice, and merchants in villages of Suzhou and Tongzhou also did not want to increase their holdings. Buyers wanted to reduce prices, resulting in a stalemate and sluggish transactions between both parties. The digestion of arrivals of thin-husked rice from the southern merchants continued sluggishly. Prices of better qualities remained stable, while those of lower qualities were still being evaluated. Demand for Yang-Du indica rice was dull, but because of the thinness of both stored and new rice, prices did not rise or fall. Both lower and better qualities of Bai-Yuan rice had some movement, and the situation had turned around, with the market trending tighter.

Yesterday, the foreign rice market was weak in the morning, with spot rice slightly declining by small fractions. In the afternoon, due to tightening futures prices, spot prices also strengthened. Foreign rice futures were supported by the belief among foreign firms that production costs were high, and they were reluctant to sell, with few recycled goods being offered. Near and far terms of Western rice improved by three or four points in small fractions, but trading volume was not high, with a total of only several thousand bags. Spot rice saw only small fractions, with 1,500 bags traded at prices ranging from 13.32 to 13.17 yuan. Other types were not actively traded. However, two ships carrying Saigon rice and other varieties are expected to arrive in Shanghai today or tomorrow, one of which is the "In-Ren-Maru," carrying over 20,000 bags, which has already arrived at the Songkou port.

Flour Market Plummets and Slightly Recovers 192

Yesterday, after the opening of the flour market in the morning, each month exhibited a pattern of sharp decline followed by a slight recovery. At the beginning of the month, because of the slight decline in the price of imported wheat, the lowest price reached 2 taels, 4 qian, and 8 and a half fen, down another small fen from the previous day. However, for March and later months, although the opening prices were also lower, speculators covering short positions and mainland merchants believed that the current market value had already fallen by 1 qian and 3 or 4 fen, or 1 qian and 6 or 7 fen, from the highest point. In terms of the extent of the decline, it was already considerable, and in terms of market value, it should be able to hold its ground. Therefore, buying interest revived, and the market stabilized. When the afternoon session opened, the prices for March through May were generally fluctuating, but the market sentiment had turned stable. For new flour for June and July, because manufacturers were not selling, the sentiment of outsiders was quite good, and the prices were particularly strong. If there are no special changes in imported wheat and the situation returns to peace, this kind of market value should not fall excessively. As a result, the price for the current month recovered by 2 li and a half from the previous day, March improved by 5 li, April by 7 li and a half, May by 1 fen and 7 li and a half, June by 1 fen and a half, and July by 1 fen and 2 li and a half.

Art World

Recent Dutch Literary Scene: New Works by Dutch Female Novelists 199

--Manru

Since ancient times, literature has been the mirror of life. This is universally acknowledged. However, literature not only reflects life, but also has some influence on it. Therefore, we can add that life influences literature, and literature also influences life. This is especially true in modern times. If we want to know the living conditions and national psychology of a certain country, the best way is to look at the artistic works of that country. The understanding we gain from such works is often more accurate and concise than the impressions we get from traveling there.

Because most of the books published in the Netherlands recently deal with issues of sexuality, failed marriages, divorce, and free love experiments, we can conclude that the question of whether the existing marriage laws are appropriate and whether men and women are truly monogamous beings has arisen in the Netherlands. Such questions are common in recent Dutch novels, and some even offer answers. This shows that sex, love, and marriage are currently the most important issues for the Dutch.

Although the Netherlands is not a large country and does not have many writers, it has quite a few female writers, especially in the field of novels. The achievements of female writers are excellent. Recently, four female writers published four full-length novels, which is a noteworthy event in the recent Dutch literary scene. Three of them focus on love, marriage, and family issues. From these three, we can see the attitudes, opinions, and solutions of Dutch women towards these issues. Now, let's talk about the content of these four novels.

The first female novelist is Mrs. Van Ammers Kuller. In her latest work, "Tantalus," she tells the story of a couple with three children who seem to be happy. The novel is titled "Tantalus" because the husband is like Tantalus in Greek mythology. Tantalus was the son of Zeus and lived in the heavenly palace. Later, because he was too arrogant, he angered the gods and was thrown into hell, immersed in a lake. When he was thirsty and wanted to drink, the water suddenly became shallow. When he was hungry and wanted to pick the fruit above his head, the fruit suddenly rose. Therefore, he was always looking at things that were desirable but unattainable, and was always hungry and thirsty. Our male protagonist is also such a character. Although his wife is beautiful, gentle, and loyal, he always feels unsatisfied and hungry. Unfortunately, he is like that unlucky Tantalus. When he sees water and wants to drink it, the water recedes. When he sees fruit and wants to eat it, the fruit moves away. He endured such pain for a long time, but never gave up. Therefore, when he later encountered delicious fruit, and the fruit was stuffed into his mouth by someone who wanted him to eat it, he quickly swallowed it. But he didn't expect to eat rotten fruit. The young woman didn't have good intentions in seducing him. Thus, this man, who was already forty and whose hair was a bit gray, made himself a laughing stock, and besides physical satisfaction, he felt deeply disappointed.

This is a beautiful novel, especially because it depicts the wife's sorrow and despair very well, without being excessive or insufficient. Although this novel is not as good as her masterpiece "The Rebel Generation," it can still calmly and objectively depict the mentality, life, and misfortunes caused by desires of modern people, without suggesting remedies or solutions.

The story of "Tantalus" only raises a question: if a husband does something wrong to his wife, should they divorce or continue to live together? The author does not give us an answer, but "Daughters" is different. It not only writes about divorce, but also provides a solution. "Daughters" is written by Carl Van Lidth Jeude. What she focuses on is not the issue of divorce, but the tragic consequences of divorce for children. When parents act selfishly and divorce at will, the happiness of their children is destroyed, and they do not consider the misfortunes that their children will suffer in the future. In the author's opinion, this is a very painful thing. Therefore, she uses this situation as the center and writes a serious and realistic novel. Moreover, in the novel, she gives a solution to this problem.

The story involves a divorced couple, and their daughters live separately. One follows her father and enjoys absolute freedom to continue her studies. The other follows her mother and grandmother and lives a domestic life. However, her mother is devoted to charity and social work, so she does not discipline her much. Therefore, she lives a free life. Like those divorced women, everyone is free and financially independent, but everyone cannot find happiness. The grandmother watches coldly and observes this group of new women and their new personalities. She feels that the pace of life of this younger generation is faster, their actions are freer, and their ideas are more progressive. However... she feels that everything is still the same in essence, with no change.

One daughter gets married and has children, but suddenly discovers that her husband is flirting with a young girl. She feels that this is intolerable and decides to separate from him. Another daughter, however, falls in love with a married man who is twenty years older than her and already has children. However, he is willing to divorce his wife to marry her. At this point, the plot of the story becomes complicated. At this time, there are two more groups of children who are about to be driven out of the family. But suddenly there is a big turning point. One of the two daughters suddenly understands what is about to happen. So the two sisters go abroad together, and in the fresh mountain air, they thoroughly discuss this issue. Their conclusion is that parents cannot be too selfish and should think about their children. Therefore, sacrificing for the sake of children is something they should do. After they come up with a solution, they return. One still goes back to reconcile with her husband, trying to forgive him and win back his love. The other rejects her lover.

This solution is of course the answer that the author gives us, but it is difficult to say whether this answer is correct. However, the situations in different countries are different, the situations in different eras are different, and the situations of different people are different. What is suitable for one is often not suitable for another. If you encounter this kind of problem, the best way is to create your own answer. What the author says is just the author's answer.

Calry Van Bruggen, in "Eve," tells the story of a woman named Eve. Eve has experienced everything that can happen in life, but she still finds life mysterious. She never understands life. As a young girl, she feels different from other girls, but she does not dare to be different. She loves beauty, loves family, especially her twin brother. But she often lives in her own fantasy world, afraid to touch the secrets of adults. When she reaches the period of flirting and sexual awakening, she is even more confused. When a young man whistles to her at night to ask her to go out, she is unwilling to listen, but she goes out to meet him. When he kisses her in a dark garden, she is suddenly filled with ecstasy, but when he roughly touches her, she runs away. However, she now understands why girls all love to go to dark gardens. Is this kind of thing right or wrong? She frantically and hastily reads a lot of books, wanting to discover from the books what the other side of love is. Then she finds the answer from Frederik Van Eeden (one of the greatest Dutch poets and prose writers). Van Eeden says,

Only that love which, in the highest joy, is stronger than all the ideals of the soul, can make carnal desire beautiful. Without that highest joy, all physical desires are merely filthy, despicable, immoral licentiousness. She regards this sentence as the golden rule, and she never forgets this sentence in her life. She gets married, has children, and feels that she is a mother, not a wife. So when her husband tells her that he loves another woman, they separate like friends. She is very satisfied to have children. But she becomes mysterious again. She does not know what place she occupies in life. She is ranked among the "noble middle-aged ladies", but she feels that she is neither noble, nor middle-aged, nor a lady. So, just when she believes that she has ended all absurd things after having two grown children, she suddenly discovers that she has truly fallen in love with a man for the first time in her life, and only this time. Until now, she realizes that there is no room for fear and shame in love. In love, there is only passion and courage. Until now, she realizes that Van Eeden's theory is a fallacious theory.

This is indeed a very unusual work, and it is different from the author's previous works. The author's previous works were often delicate and philosophical, but "Eve" was written in a moment of inspiration, with unpretentious prose. However, even so, this novel is very active and fluent, and it analyzes a woman's psychology very exquisitely and sincerely. Furthermore, this novel can also be said to be the autobiography of this female novelist. She was the pioneer of the Dutch "modern girl", cutting her hair short and walking on the street without a hat. She was the first one. Those who know her past life can easily find traces of her in this novel.

The above three are centered on marriage and love, but Mathile A Van BJLaen's "Island of Forgetfulness" is completely different from these three. This is the winning novel in the previous Dutch prize-winning competition. Among the two hundred or so anonymous entries, this novel won first place. However, unfortunately, its author passed away before the prize was announced. She was still a young female writer.

This is a novel about post-war life, obviously written because the author witnessed many post-war tragedies. The book roughly says that a doctor in British India obtains a secret medicine, taking it causes people to lose their memory. Because many people cannot forget the tragedies of the past and suffer pain in their hearts, this kind doctor wants to use this medicine to make them forget everything. He later actually finds some of these poor people (the book tells their individual stories), and takes them to a desert island. Everyone drinks this medicine juice at the same time, and the medicine is indeed effective. They forget all their past and no longer remember their sorrows. Then, their life should be happy and happy, but it is not. Their thinking power still exists. They gradually become surprised and eager to understand where they came from. Later, they learn that they have taken a kind of medicine. So everyone feels that the truth, even if it is terrible, is always better than groping in the dark without knowing anything. So they force the doctor to give them some antidote to restore them to their original state. The doctor cannot deal with them, but luckily he has an antidote, so he gives them the antidote. These people have since fallen into the sea of sorrow again.

The idea of this novel is very novel, but unfortunately the technique is worse, the style is also dry and clumsy, and the ability of this medicine shows flaws, which is not easy to cause the reader to believe. This is the author's lack of talent. Although the whole book is quite era-specific,

Theater News 200

Central to Screen Famous German Film

The Central Company declares that German films tend to emphasize ideals, especially the pursuit of material civilization in the future, unlike American films, which focus solely on love without any basis, and intentionally attack the weaknesses of foreign countries. The Central Company has not seen this in German films. For example, German film works during the European War had no political odor. Most works adopted the essence of mythology and art. Therefore, knowledgeable people in various countries also praised the German film industry for its contribution to improving humanity through art. Recently, the most valuable films screened in Shanghai are "Scientific World" and "Absurd Love". The former has a religious background, and the latter has an ethical background, and the key is the mystery of artificial humans, and the creator temporarily loses his ambition and wants to deceive the created person. Eventually, he is harmed by the created person. Its punishment of evil and warning to the world are one and the same. The grandeur of the background in the film and the exquisite coloring and engraving are especially praised by the art world. It is said that this film will be continuously screened at the Central Grand Theater for three days starting from March 1.

Paris Premiere of "Iron Heel Red Dance" a Sensation

The Paris Grand Theater declares that yesterday, the first day of the world-shaking Russian Revolution love epic "Iron Heel Red Dance" premiered at this theater. All three shows, day and night, were sold out upstairs and downstairs. Many people were turned away due to late arrival. The plot and scenery of the drama can be called unparalleled, and the American socialite's stage performance of "Red Dance" is very sensual, and the audience is very satisfied.

Publishing News 201

Yu Nairen's Famous Work Published

Mr. Yu Nairen, from Kaifeng, Henan, studied in Europe for many years. After returning to China, he successively held important military and political positions in the National Government. He has long been respected by elders at home and abroad. Last winter, he recuperated in Shanghai and released his old manuscript "A Glimpse of European Military Affairs After the War."

After sorting it out, he entrusted it to the printer. It has now become a book and is published. The contents of the book include detailed and magnificent records of the current situation, military agencies, military organization, organization education, strength statistics, and military expenditure of various countries such as France, Germany, Italy, and Russia after the war. It is a truly great contribution and can serve as a reference for national defense and the only reference book for military and political figures.

Youth Corner

Secret Diary 202

— Sunflower

Speaking out for Young Men and Women

I have lived past sixteen years old, I am getting old. I have lived through the two most beautiful ages. In anyone's life history, the so-called wonderful age of youth is only the two ages of fifteen and sixteen.

Ah, why do parents, teachers, and elders in society generally lock up young men and women who are at the age of wonderfulness, and confine them in a box-like world? Why force them to stay away from nature, away from the forest, away from happiness? Why strictly forbid them from interacting with young people of the opposite sex?

Why only teach them boring and useless courses, but not enlighten ordinary young men and women with interesting and beneficial literature and art, or common sense about physiological health?

Why only tirelessly explain the methods of mathematics and the principles of philosophy, but not mention a word about the methods of love and the principles of marriage that are closely related to the youth that will never return?

Do you think that the age of youth is not worth cherishing, that youth will come back after it is gone, that human beings can have two sixteen-year-olds? Please read the following two sentences:

Fifteen years old is the age when a woman leaves her childhood, leaves the hands of the creator, how innocent and pure.

What do you think after reading this? Aren't you going to examine your conscience? Ah, your wonderful age has been ravaged by your enforcers. Although you now deeply regret it, or resent it, time will never return, and it is too late.

Why use gender to separate young people? Why forbid them from socializing? Finally, I want to ask you, why must you first make them marry before you are willing to let young men associate with young women, or let young women associate with young men?

Ah, the world is so beautiful, and human beings are so intelligent. The creator puts young men and women together, calling them to love and rejoice with each other from morning to night, from night to morning. One look from one of them can make the other happy. Just a lock of hair can be preserved for ten years. Just one kiss contributes the entire life. This is truly a wonderful, beautiful, and fragrant sweet dream. This seems to be a special right that can be enjoyed in youth.

However, social figures insist on destroying it, saying something like "These children's love cannot last long, and they should be corrected, and they must not be allowed to indulge in love." So people isolate them, closing him or her alone in a desolate bedroom or study, using all means to destroy their youth. The man is told to study, and the woman is told to sew. The books that people give to young women to read are all unimportant moral cultivation textbooks, until she marries a husband, then they say to her, "From now on, you can read whatever you want." Then she naturally chooses to read novels. Her favorite things to read are the works of Zola and Maupassant.

God, if I could live with a girl of my age, have a girl to worship, a lover, how happy I would be. I would willingly hold her neck for the rest of my life, my head resting on her chest, my lips touching her cheeks, her hair covering my eyes...

Ah, woman, woman, I am already seventeen years old, I have never tasted a kiss of love, never heard a word of love, never seen a smile. Ah, I am going to burn, I am going to burn!

Ah, every dusk, I sleep alone in bed, tossing and turning unable to sleep. Every time I imagine that my dream lover is sleeping next to me, everyone cuddling together, I caress her, she comforts me, without any evil thoughts. Ah, I only see her face, her hair, her head, the rest is just a blurry shadow. We talk lovingly, and the scent of love emanates from her body. I am drunk... My bed becomes the Garden of Eden. But when I wake up the next morning, I am just one person, feeling more lonely than before, my heart is tight, my tongue is dry, and my spirit is sad. Ah, please don't laugh at me, some of you must have the same illness as me. Ah, when I am now writing these lines, my mind is still uneasy. Perhaps there is a lovely sixteen-year-old girl who is also writing the same boredom and loneliness as me in her diary. She is thirsting to find a young man like me.

It is also unknowable...

Ahem, ahem, I can't write anymore, I'm going to cry.

Excerpted and translated from "Secret Diary" by Pierre Louÿs (Diary of October 10, 1887)

Page 25

Social News

Urban Sketches Lin 203

(3) Going to the Vegetable Market

Everyone, directly or indirectly, has some relationship with the vegetable market, from simple meals of rice and greens to elaborate banquets with delicacies. From entering the throat to the stomach, and then from the stomach to fertilizer, in this great cycle, you can't escape the process of the vegetable market. In the vegetable market, we can see all kinds of flora and fauna, such as vegetables, fish, meat, shrimp, crabs, shellfish, etc. Different things have different colors and inconsistent smells. Green, yellow, red, white, black, sweet, sour, bitter, spicy, salty, everything is available, all-encompassing. The vegetable market is like a miniature society, intricate and complex, with the most members, and different in price and distinct in class. Those who study social science must have a deep understanding of the economic organization and material distribution in society in order to understand the origin of various realities in society. We go to the vegetable market, and we want to study the philosophy in the vegetable market.

For women, going to the vegetable market is like going to the battlefield. The vegetable vendors in the vegetable market are naturally "waiting in battle." It is not surprising to argue over a few copper coins or a few vegetables. They are meticulous and not afraid of trouble in choosing vegetables and picking fish and meat. Eyes, nose, and fingers are used together to make a final decision. As for the price, it is more important than the material. Customers ask each other about prices, just like inquiring about military intelligence. The vegetable vendors bargaining with customers is like issuing a challenge, with verbal battles and endless noise. By the time things are bought, the spirit is almost gone. That's probably why there is such a loud noise in every vegetable market when it opens.

When you walk through the vegetable market, you may as well slow down and observe for five minutes. The vegetable vendors stand behind their stalls, their eyes looking either into the customers' baskets or into their own baskets, their mouths shouting, and their hands moving continuously. This is nothing more than the meaning of promotion and attracting customers. For example, the vegetable vendor selling radishes often turns the vegetable basket, picks the largest and fattest radishes, and throws them in his palm. Most of the fish on the fish stall are out of breath. The fish vendors also roll up their sleeves and reach into the water to fish. In fact, reaching into the water can at least get two or three fish. However, he circled several times in the water bucket, and then tightly grasped a fish, as if the fish was about to jump away. When it came out of the water, it was still splashing around. This is nothing more than indicating to customers that the fish is "alive." In fact, the meaning of "lively" in the fish vendor's mouth is "no action, no jump."

As for the customers who buy vegetables, the expressions on their faces have various changes. For example, a woman wants to buy bamboo shoots. When she passes the bamboo shoot stall, she slows down, looks into the bamboo shoot basket, and asks the price after a while. At this time, her expression at least contains a sign of hope. If the price asked by the bamboo shoot vendor is too high or surprisingly cheap, the expression on her face will change again. Once the price is agreed upon, she will start to pick and choose. If the head of a bamboo shoot is too long and too old, she will usually ask the bamboo shoot vendor to cut it off. Since the bamboo shoot vendor cuts off too much, the weight will be reduced, and he cannot buy more money. So he cuts off a corner thinly. The woman disagrees and must ask him to cut off more. At this time, there is a major change on her face, because the principle of economics is the simplest, and other people's cheapness is her own loss, so she must be cautious. The last step is to pay. Copper coins are like bullets, and there is no reason to misfire one.

From six or seven o'clock in the morning until nine or ten o'clock in the morning, people in the vegetable market are busy coming in and out. Bright colors and fishy smells are sent to people at the same time. There are pleasing green and red colors, natural earthy smells, terrible flesh and blood, and discordant fishy smells. The ground in the vegetable market is always wet for ten out of ten days. The air inside is more turbid than clean. The wooden shelves for displaying vegetables and the bamboo baskets for storing vegetables are the only utensils in the vegetable market. When it is not yet dawn, under the deep yellow light, many vegetable vendors carry their goods and rush to the vegetable market. Not much

In a moment, the thin and bony shelves will be piled

Page 26

Quite a lot of meat and fish. Later, more and more people gathered, and the wooden shelves were gradually hidden. After lunch, those pairs of shelves still exposed their bones to people.

Except when there is a vegetable market, there is no fun in the vegetable market. The cold cement floor is wet in one place and dry in another. There is no decoration around except for the pillars. However, it is very different in the morning. Different things are displayed, placed horizontally, placed vertically, piled up, and laid flat, each different. Some people manage seven or eight baskets, and some have other things besides a pile of shallots and ginger. As for the hawkers selling household goods, they also borrow the vegetable market as their base camp. In addition, there are many pawn shops, southern goods stores, and ham stores opened near the vegetable market. There are so many shops that are incidentally produced by the vegetable market that it is impossible to say them all at once. However, the opening of matchmaker shops near the vegetable market indirectly contains a direct meaning, which is definitely not accidental.

There are no less than thirty or forty vegetable markets in the whole city of Shanghai. Taking the public concession alone, there are thirteen or fourteen places such as Hongkou, Xinzha, Avenue Edward VII, Huishan, East Hongkou, Rue Marco Polo, Boone Road, North Fujian Road, Wuzhou Road, Songpan Road, and Yangshupu. The number of vegetable stalls totals about four or five thousand. The stall donations collected by the Municipal Council in various vegetable markets every year are nearly 200,000 yuan, which is quite considerable. Ordinary vegetable markets are only on flat ground, and larger ones have one or two floors, mostly cement buildings. The iron house vegetable market on Nanjing Road sells some "raw Western vegetables". The Hongkou vegetable market has the most variety, telling us that there are many places with international flavors.

The situation in the vegetable market varies in four seasons. There is also a seasonal relationship between vegetables, fish, and meat. The vegetable market tells us about the change of climate, and also tells us about the social situation. As for the merits of the municipal administration and the habits of the residents, the vegetable market is an excellent "information center".

Statistics on the Japanese Chicken Industry 204

48 Million Chickens Raised

Egg Production Worth 80 Million Yuan

According to the Japanese Ministry of Agriculture and Forestry, as of the end of June last year, the number of chicken farmers in Japan was 3,438,622, a decrease of 31,178 households from the previous year. There were a total of 48,257,620 chickens, worth 44,316,358 yuan. The total output in the year before the end of June last year was 253,172,9569 eggs, worth 88,904,450 yuan.

The Fastest Flying Insect 205

Liang Xiongwan

In the world, if there really is an insect that can fly 850 miles per hour, it must be able to make long-distance flights without having to stop midway. At four o'clock in the morning, it can leave New York, fly around the earth in a week, and still be able to fly back to New York at nine o'clock that night. Is there really such a capable insect with such rapid flight in the world? Yes, there really is. Dr. Charles Townson recently discovered this insect, called Cehonomyia. There are very few of this kind of insects in the world, because of its rapid flight, it is indeed a difficult task to collect this kind of insect, and the number of Cehonomyia that have been collected is only a few. Multiple trials have confirmed that its rapid flight is indeed as described above. If such a rate can be obtained from artificial machinery, the speed of transportation will have an astonishing improvement. For example, if an airplane can fly 850 miles per hour, we can leave New York at four o'clock in the morning, have breakfast in Reno, have lunch in Beijing, have a snack in Constantinople, have dinner in Madrid, and may be able to fly back to New York at nine o'clock in the same afternoon.

This Cehonomyia insect can fly around the earth in a week in seventeen hours. Its body is as big as a large bee, and its speed per hour is three times the speed of an ordinary airplane.

Germany's Passion Play 206

Bi Tian

Speaking of the Oberammergau Passion Play in Bavaria, Germany, it is extremely famous in Europe. This kind of Passion Play has been staged for 300 years, but it is not staged every year. The custom is to perform it once every ten years, and there is only a preview in ordinary years. This year happens to be the year of performance. In Europe, such news must have been very noisy.

This Passion Play is entirely performed by ordinary people - merchants, farmers, workers and people of all classes. However, because there is a preview once a year, the skills of the actors have also been tempered to a considerable extent, but it is naturally different from professional actors. The performance is full of plainness, purity, and piety, and can hold the audience's hearts. The roles of Jesus and the Virgin Mary are determined by the general villagers' vote. The time is from May to August, twice a week, and there are a total of thirty-two performances. The theater is an extension of the original theater, with about 5,200 seats. Seat reservations have probably been booked, and about 80% of the total number is occupied by Americans.
